Stage 2 raises `PaymentRequired` if `state.payment.paid == False` when attempted — operational safety, not an agent cap.
- `run.py`: single `run_audit(slug, target_stage=None)` function that loops through stage functions and calls them in order.
- Workspace layout: `clients/<slug>/audit/{intake,cache,prediscovery,agents,synthesis,proposal,deliverable,walkthrough}/` + `state.json` + `cost_log.jsonl`. (R3 restructure 2026-04-22: Stage-2 working directory renamed `lenses/` → `agents/` — each Stage-2 agent writes to `agents/<agent>/` instead of `lenses/<lens>/`; 7 agents produce findings tagged with `report_section` Literal enum that route to 9 report sections in Stage 3 synthesis. **R5 addition 2026-04-22**: `cache/` subdirectory holds tool-handler cache files keyed by `<tool_name>_<sha256(args)[:12]>.json`, 24h TTL, eval-fixture substrate.)
- Atomic state writes: `state.json.tmp` → rename → `git add && git commit`.

**Test scenarios:**
- Happy: fresh workspace + `freddy audit run` populates state.json and commits.
- Happy: `freddy audit run --stage 3` resumes at stage 3 only.
- Happy: `state.sessions[<role>].session_id` populated after any Claude Agent SDK call completes; subsequent resume uses it.
- Happy: `record_payment(state, stripe_event)` sets `state.payment.paid = True` and persists via atomic rename + git commit.
- Edge: running `freddy audit run --stage 2` with `state.payment.paid == False` raises `PaymentRequired` with message pointing JR to `freddy audit send-invoice` and `freddy audit mark-paid`.
- Edge: corrupted state.json raises actionable error with `--reset` hint.
- Happy: `content_extractor.extract(url)` returns non-empty result for HTML, PDF, YouTube URLs.

**Done when:** `freddy client new test --url https://example.com && freddy audit run --client test` produces valid empty workspace + state.json with all stages pending + one git commit.

---

### U2. Pre-discovery primitives (R5 2026-04-22: ~2 local-only Python helpers + 6 cache-backed SDK tool handlers + ~75 prompt-mention investigations)

**R5 reframing of U2 (2026-04-22):** Earlier R3+R4 plan called for ~83 Python wrapper functions in `primitives.py` + 12 new modules in `src/audit/providers/`. Pressure-testing surfaced that ~68 of these are `WebFetch(url) + extract + judge` shells around free public APIs — work the agent does natively. R5 collapses U2 to:

- **~15 owned-provider tool handlers** under `src/audit/tools/` (~300 LOC total, see new U2.5 below): `dataforseo_tool` (8 endpoints) + `cloro_tool.ai_visibility` + `competitive_tool.ads` (Foreplay+Adyntel via existing CompetitiveAdService) + `monitoring_tool` (dispatches to 12 existing adapters) + `gsc_tool` (when attached). Each is cache-aware: read cache → return on hit; provider-call → write cache → return on miss. **Zero new provider modules** — handlers wrap existing wired providers (`src/seo/providers/*`, `src/geo/providers/*`, `src/competitive/*`, `src/monitoring/adapters/*`).
- **~2 local-only Python helpers** in `src/audit/primitives.py`: `fingerprint_martech_stack()` (wappalyzer-next + `data/martech_rules.yaml` regex/JS-fingerprint extension) and `content_strategy_embeddings_cluster()` (text-embedding-3-small + k-means for content-pillar clustering). Both run locally without network; not appropriate for SDK-tool exposure.
- **~68 free-public-API investigations** become **prompt-mention instructions** in the Stage-1 pre-discovery agent prompt (`PREDISCOVERY_PROMPT`) and the 7 Stage-2 agent prompts (`AGENT_*_PROMPT`). Each prompt names: target URL pattern, auth pattern, polite pace, pagination pattern, expected response shape, and the rubric the data feeds. Agent uses WebFetch / `cli/scripts/fetch_api.sh` (curl-with-retry) to execute. **No Python wrapper exists for**: GitHub REST/GraphQL, Wikipedia/Lift Wing, SEC EDGAR, HuggingFace Hub, Reddit OAuth, Product Hunt GraphQL, crt.sh, Firefox AMO, Atlassian Marketplace, MediaWiki, GDELT, Discord Invite, Podchaser, APIs.guru, Mailinator/disposable-email, Mail-Tester, Mozilla HTTP Observatory, npm registry, PyPI JSON, Greenhouse/Lever/Ashby/Workable ATS APIs, Wayback CDX, Bluesky AT Protocol, axe-playwright accessibility (run via Playwright in agent context, no wrapper).
- **5 safety-bounded primitives** (Tier D — `audit_welcome_email_signup`, `audit_hiring_funnel_ux`, R23 `attach-demo`, R21 `attach-survey` PII handling, R22 `attach-assets` IP) require capability restriction via `src/audit/scoped_tools.py`. The capability restriction code is the only "primitive wrapper" code that must exist for safety reasons; agent cannot bypass via prompt-mention because the destructive capability isn't in its toolbelt at all.

**The per-primitive specs that follow** (preserved from R3+R4 plans for coverage reference) describe **what each rubric/signal must produce**, not "this must be a Python function." Read every spec below as: agent investigation target named in prompt + which tool handler or WebFetch reaches the data + what signals must surface in findings. The previous Python-function framing is superseded — the coverage requirements are not.

**Goal (R5 reframed):** Stage-1 pre-discovery agent + 7 Stage-2 agents + 2 local helpers + 6 cache-backed tool handlers cover the same signal surface area as R3+R4's 83 Python functions, with the agent layer producing the WebFetch/Bash work directly per prompt-mention instructions.

**Original framing (R3+R4, superseded but preserved as coverage reference):** All ~83 functions in a single `src/audit/primitives.py` file — plus a shared Playwright fetcher and 12 net-new shared providers under `src/audit/providers/`. Each primitive is a Python function returning a TypedDict, graceful degradation with `partial: bool` on all of them. Split:
- **Primitives 1–9 (original baseline)**: `tech_stack`, `enumerate_subdomains`, `scrape_careers`, `scrape_firmographics`, `detect_schema`, `score_ai_visibility`, `scan_competitor_pages`, `gather_voc`, `detect_analytics_tags` (note: `detect_analytics_tags` is being superseded by `fingerprint_martech_stack` below — see the P25 supersedes-note).
- **Primitives 10–18 (SaaS-parity)**: `analyze_backlinks`, `audit_page_speed`, `historical_rank_trends`, `keyword_gap_analysis`, `analyze_serp_features`, `analyze_internal_links`, `audit_on_page_seo`, `audit_content_quality`, `estimate_traffic` — cover Ahrefs / SEMrush / PageSpeed Insights / Screaming Frog / Similarweb.
- **Primitives 19–25 (full-agency coverage, Option B)**: `enumerate_brand_social_handles`, `audit_channel_presence`, `audit_youtube_channel`, `audit_podcast_footprint`, `capture_surface_scan`, `deliverability_posture`, `fingerprint_martech_stack` — close the Distribution / Lifecycle / MarTech-Attribution gap vs a full-service agency audit.
- **Primitives 26–30 (Brand/Narrative coverage, Option C)**: `audit_messaging_consistency`, `audit_executive_visibility`, `audit_content_strategy_shape`, `audit_earned_media_footprint`, `audit_partnership_event_community_footprint` — close the brand / thought-leadership / PR-narrative / community / partnerships / events gap.
- **Primitive 31 (conditional ASO)**: `audit_aso` — runs only when `scrape_firmographics` detects a mobile app. App Store + Play Store listing quality + review velocity + keyword rank. **Extended 2026-04-22**: 6-dimension weighted rubric (Title 20% / Description 15% / Visual 25% / Ratings 20% / Metadata 10% / Conversion 10%) + brand-maturity tier adjustment (Dominant >10M reviews / Established 100K-10M / Challenger <100K) + desktop marketplaces (Mac App Store via `parseforge/mac-app-store-scraper` Apify actor + Microsoft Store via RenderedFetcher + Setapp catalog scrape).
- **Primitives 32–48 (audit-coverage research expansion, 2026-04-22)**: net-new collection primitives across all 9 lenses + 2 conditional firmographic primitives. Listed individually below; full per-primitive signals/sources/cost/confidence dossiers in `docs/plans/2026-04-22-002-audit-coverage-research.md`.
  - **SEO + Site Quality (5)**: `audit_international_seo` (P32, conditional multi-locale), `audit_local_seo` (P33, conditional local-business), `audit_accessibility` (P34, unconditional), `audit_help_center_docs` (P35, conditional SaaS with thin path for others), `audit_pricing_page` (P36, unconditional, with localization sub-signals when multi-locale).
  - **Distribution + Listings (5)**: `audit_directory_presence` (P37, unconditional + AI-firmographic subset for TAAFT/Futurepedia), `audit_marketplace_listings` (P38, unconditional), `audit_launch_cadence` (P39, unconditional), `audit_free_tools` (P40, unconditional), `audit_oss_footprint` (P41, conditional dev-tool/tech firmographic).
  - **Brand / Narrative / Customer (4)**: `audit_customer_education` (P42, unconditional), `audit_public_roadmap` (P43, unconditional), `audit_corporate_responsibility` (P44, conditional mid-market+ to avoid SMB false-negatives), `audit_customer_story_program` (P45, unconditional).
  - **Conversion / Trust / Funnel / ABM (3)**: `audit_trust_signals` (P46, unconditional), `audit_funnel_content_shape` (P47, unconditional, severity-cap=low — descriptive content/CTA shape, NOT a velocity claim), `audit_abm_signals` (P48, conditional B2B-enterprise firmographic).
- **Conditional firmographic primitives (2 net-new in R1 expansion)**: `audit_plg_motion` (conditional SaaS firmographic — pure_freemium / free_trial / reverse_trial / hybrid classification + viral mechanism scoring), `audit_devex` (conditional dev-tool firmographic — docs platform tier + OpenAPI discoverability + SDK coverage + npm/PyPI freshness).
- **Primitives 49–80 (audit-coverage research expansion R2, 2026-04-22 second pass)**: 32 net-new collection primitives + ~24 deepening extensions across all 9 lenses + 2 net-new reasoning primitives. Listed individually below; full per-primitive signals/sources/cost/confidence dossiers in `docs/plans/2026-04-22-003-audit-coverage-research-r2.md`.
  - **SEO + GEO + Compliance (12 — Group A)**: `audit_eeat_signals` (P49), `audit_robots_strategic` (P50), `audit_crawl_budget_bloat` (P51), `audit_conversational_query_optimization` (P52, renamed from voice-search), `audit_vertical_compliance` (P53, conditional vertical), `audit_ai_policy` (P54), `audit_sustainability_carbon` (P55, sub of `audit_corporate_responsibility`); plus 5 deepening extensions (footer optimization sub of `audit_on_page_seo`, documentation translations sub of `audit_help_center_docs`, sub-processor/DPA sub of `audit_trust_signals`, anchor-text branded-vs-commercial sub of `analyze_backlinks`, schema competitive comparison reasoning).
  - **Brand + Narrative + PR (13 — Group B, after diversity-imagery REJECTED)**: `audit_branded_serp` (P56), `audit_branded_autosuggest` (P57), `audit_industry_analyst_position` (P58 — single largest remaining B2B SaaS finding; Gartner MQ Leader drives 30-50% enterprise close rate), `audit_clv_retention_signals` (P59); plus 9 deepening extensions (newsletter quality + research depth + leaderboard rank subs of `audit_content_strategy_shape`; owned-podcast quality sub of `audit_podcast_footprint`; rebrand history Wayback + brand voice cross-platform subs of `audit_messaging_consistency`; wire-vs-original press ratio + M&A history subs of `audit_earned_media_footprint`; comments engagement sub of `audit_partnership_event_community_footprint`; brand demand trend sub of `gather_voc`).
  - **Conversion + Trust + Funnel + Sales (12 — Group C)**: `audit_customer_support` (P60), `audit_cro_experimentation_maturity` (P61), `audit_ecommerce_catalog` (P62, conditional DTC/e-comm), `audit_b2c_personalization` (P63, conditional B2C/DTC), `audit_homepage_demo_video` (P64), `audit_first_party_data_strategy` (P65), `audit_trust_center` (P66), `audit_sales_motion_classification` (P67, reasoning-only synthesis), `audit_mobile_ux` (P68); plus 3 deepening extensions (push notification opt-in sub of `capture_surface_scan`, cross-sell/upsell sub of conversion lens, paywall-upgrade-cro sub of `audit_pricing_page` when freemium detected).
  - **Distribution + Community + Partnerships (12 — Group D)**: `audit_mobile_app_linking` (P69, conditional mobile-app + flag dead Firebase Dynamic Links), `audit_reddit_ama_brand_subreddit` (P70), `audit_influencer_ftc_compliance` (P71, conditional influencer mentions), `audit_hackathon_dev_event_sponsorships` (P72, conditional dev-tool), `audit_branded_merchandise_swag` (P73), `audit_customer_advisory_board_references` (P74, conditional B2B), `audit_university_academic_partnerships` (P75, conditional research-heavy/dev-tool/edtech), `audit_ctv_ads_detection` (P76, LOW-confidence degraded — primary value is "pointer to upgrade path" via R20), `audit_apple_search_ads` (P77, conditional mobile-app + R20 ad-platform enrichment), `audit_geographic_expansion` (P78); plus 3 deepening extensions (status page maturity sub of `audit_partnership_event_community_footprint`, newsletter leaderboard rank sub of `audit_content_strategy_shape`, swag/CAB/university subs of partnership_event_community_footprint).
  - **Specialized + Infrastructure + Operations (8 — Group E)**: `audit_email_signature_marketing_indicators` (P79, MEDIUM-LOW confidence triangulation; emit only when ≥2 weak signals concur), `audit_error_page_ux` (P80), `audit_open_api_public_data_access` (P81, with ProgrammableWeb dropped + RapidAPI declining flagged), `audit_github_discussions_volume` (P82, conditional Discussions enabled), `audit_huggingface_presence` (P83, conditional AI firmographic), `audit_welcome_email_signup` (P84, conditional free-trial/freemium detected + **manual user opt-in flag** — see safety pattern below), `audit_public_company_ir` (P85, conditional public-company firmographic), `audit_hiring_funnel_ux` (P86, conditional ATS detected — never submit application form per safety pattern).
- **Reasoning primitives (3 total)**: `assess_attribution_maturity` (P2a, derived from `fingerprint_martech_stack` + `analyze_internal_links`), **`audit_sales_motion_classification`** (P67, derived from `audit_pricing_page` + `scrape_careers` + `capture_surface_scan` + `tech_stack` outbound-tool detection — outputs `motion_type ∈ {plg, inside_sales, enterprise_sales, hybrid_plg_to_sales, hybrid_smb_to_enterprise}`), **`audit_schema_competitive`** (synthesis pass comparing prospect schema to top 3 competitors).

All new primitives consume **owned providers** wherever possible (see "Data provider inventory"). Net-new external sources are all free or near-free: GitHub REST/GraphQL (free with `GITHUB_TOKEN`), Product Hunt API (free), crt.sh + CertSpotter (free), Firefox AMO (free), Atlassian Marketplace REST (free), MediaWiki + Lift Wing (free), Mozilla HTTP Observatory v2 (free), ATS public job-board APIs Greenhouse/Lever/Ashby/Workable (free), npm registry + PyPI JSON (free), `axe-playwright-python` (free open-source). Two new paid dependencies: Bright Data for Glassdoor (~$0.10–0.50/audit, optional Tier-2 escalation only for >$10M revenue prospects) and Apify LinkedIn page-only scrape (~$0.05/audit, default Tier-1). Existing paid: SerpAPI, DataForSEO. Total cost delta worst-case: +$1.50–3.50/audit when all triggered; +$3–8 when R23 attach-demo (Sonnet vision) + R26 attach-winloss (transcript embeddings + clustering) also fire.

**Per-primitive specs for the 17 + 2 expansion primitives (compact form — full dossier in `2026-04-22-002-audit-coverage-research.md`):**

- **`audit_international_seo(domain, sitemap_urls)` (P32 — Phase 1, conditional multi-locale)** — Triggers when any of: `>1` distinct hreflang on homepage, ccTLD/locale subdomain in `enumerate_subdomains` output, firmographic `markets[]>1`, `/lang/` or `/<2-letter-locale>/` URL segment in sitemap. Else returns `{skipped: true, reason: "single_locale"}`. Signals: hreflang reciprocity, x-default presence + target validity, locale URL strategy (ccTLD/subdomain/subfolder/parameter), canonical-vs-hreflang conflicts, ISO 639-1/3166-1 code validity, IP-based geo-redirect blocking alt-locale indexing (Playwright with `setGeolocation`), regional sitemap presence. Sources: `dataforseo.audit_hreflang()` extension + sitemap parse + Playwright geo-render. Cost ~$0.07. Confidence HIGH.
- **`audit_local_seo(domain, brand, firmographic)` (P33 — Phase 1, conditional local-business)** — Triggers when firmographic `business_type ∈ {restaurant, retail, dental, legal, medical, contractor, gym, salon, automotive, real_estate, hospitality, professional_services_local}` OR physical-address `<address>`/`LocalBusiness` schema on homepage OR `>2` location pages on sitemap. Else `{skipped: true}`. Signals: GBP completeness via DataForSEO Business Data (no GBP API approval needed), NAP consistency across 7 high-value citation sites pulled from JSON-LD `sameAs[]` (Yelp + Apple Maps + Bing + TripAdvisor + Foursquare + YellowPages + BBB; Yelp+TripAdvisor route through Playwright due to bot-blocking), local-pack SERP rankings via `dataforseo.local_pack_serp()` for 5 city+keyword queries, geographic landing-pages depth, `LocalBusiness`/`Restaurant`/`MedicalBusiness` schema validity, service-area markup. **BrightLocal NOT required for v1** — covers 80% of finding value free; defer to Phase 2 only if local-business audits become >20% of pipeline. Cost ~$0.20. Confidence MEDIUM (high on GBP + schema, low on long-tail citation discovery).
- **`audit_accessibility(domain)` (P34 — Phase 1, unconditional)** — Audits homepage + top 3 landing pages from sitemap. Signals: Lighthouse a11y score via PageSpeed `category=accessibility` (5-LOC extension to `pagespeed.py`); axe-core violations via `axe-playwright-python` grouped by impact (critical/serious/moderate/minor) with rule IDs + sample selectors; color-contrast failures (4.5:1 normal / 3:1 large); alt-text coverage; form-label associations; landmark structure; ARIA misuse; accessibility-statement detection. **Critical: detect AccessiBe / UserWay / EqualWeb overlay scripts as NEGATIVE signal** (ADA-litigation-magnet flag — surfaces as severity=critical for US/EU sites). Sources: PageSpeed extension + axe-playwright-python + Wappalyzer overlay-vendor fingerprints. Cost ~$0.05. Confidence HIGH.
- **`audit_help_center_docs(domain, sitemap_urls, internal_links_cache)` (P35 — Phase 2, conditional SaaS+ thin path others)** — Path probes (`/help`, `/docs`, `/support`, `/knowledge-base`, `/kb`, `/learn`, `/resources/docs`, `/developers`, `/api-docs`, `/reference`) + subdomain probes from `enumerate_subdomains` output. **Algolia DocSearch detection** is the strong investment signal (CDN script `cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/@docsearch/(js|css)`, DOM `.DocSearch-Button`, `<meta name="docsearch:*">`). Other docs-platform fingerprints additive: GitBook, Mintlify, Docusaurus, ReadMe, Notion-as-docs, Document360, Zendesk Guide, Intercom Help, HelpScout Docs. Article count + median article-age + `% updated last 90d` + search-bar prominence + max nav depth + API reference presence + changelog cadence. Reuses 200-page corpus from `analyze_internal_links` when docs lives on same domain. Cost ~$0.10. Confidence HIGH.
- **`audit_pricing_page(domain, competitors[])` (P36 — Phase 2, unconditional + localization deepening when multi-locale)** — Pricing-page detection + tier extraction (regex-fallback to Sonnet for non-regex-friendly layouts; expect 70-80% extraction rate across diverse SaaS), billing-toggle detection, anchoring patterns (highlighted/recommended plan, decoy pricing, strikethrough, annual-savings copy), feature-comparison matrix, free trial / freemium signals, CTA verb diversity per tier, social proof on pricing page. **Localization deepening** (when `audit_international_seo` returned >1 locale): currency switcher detection, regional payment method icons (SEPA/iDEAL/Alipay/WeChat Pay/Boleto/OXXO/GCash/Klarna/PIX/UPI/BLIK/Bancontact via Wappalyzer + custom regex), tax-inclusive pricing copy (EU compliance), multi-currency pricing pages, geo-pricing differences (Playwright with `setGeolocation`). **Competitive pricing comparison** via 1 Cloro AI-pricing triangulation query (`compare pricing of <brand> vs <comp1> vs <comp2>`) — bands divergence as informational only since AI hallucinates prices. Cost ~$0.07. Confidence MEDIUM (high on detection, medium on tier extraction completeness).
- **`audit_directory_presence(domain, brand, firmographic)` (P37 — Phase 1, unconditional + AI-firmographic subset)** — Detects presence on G2, Capterra, GetApp, Software Advice, AlternativeTo, SaaSHub, Product Hunt history, BetaList, Chrome Web Store, Apple Developer, GitHub Marketplace via DataForSEO `serp_site_query()` for each (~$0.0006/call); Product Hunt structured data via `producthunt.py` provider. **AI-firmographic subset** (TAAFT, Futurepedia, Toolify) only fires when prospect is AI-tool firmographic. Listing-quality enrichment (claimed/unclaimed, review count, response rate) for top hits via Apify scrapers — **G2/Capterra accept "presence yes / quality unknown" disclaimer** since both are Cloudflare-protected (DataDome). AlternativeTo via Apify (`apify/alternativeto-scraper`). Chrome Web Store via Apify (`klondikeking/chrome-web-store-scraper`). Cost ~$0.15. Confidence HIGH for presence / MEDIUM for quality.
- **`audit_marketplace_listings(domain, brand)` (P38 — Phase 1, unconditional)** — Distinct from P37: platform-integration marketplaces (Zapier, Slack, Salesforce AppExchange/AgentExchange, AWS, HubSpot, Microsoft AppSource, Google Workspace, Shopify, Notion, Atlassian, Stripe). **Atlassian Marketplace REST API v3** (free, public, unauthenticated) is the only platform with clean public API — gives install count + rating + review count + app key directly via `atlassian_marketplace.py` provider. Everything else: DataForSEO `serp_site_query()` for presence (~$0.0006/call × 11 platforms) + RenderedFetcher for detail pages where DOM exposes count/rating (Shopify, AppExchange) + Apify scrapers for AWS/Slack/Stripe when listing-quality data matters. Cost ~$0.20. Confidence HIGH for presence / MEDIUM for detail.
- **`audit_launch_cadence(domain, brand)` (P39 — Phase 1, unconditional)** — Product Hunt launch history via `producthunt.py` (cadence months between launches, all-time upvotes, badges); changelog detection at `/changelog`, `/releases`, `/whats-new`, `/release-notes`, `/updates` + RSS/Atom autodiscovery from `<link rel="alternate" type="application/rss+xml">`; waitlist mechanism detection (getwaitlist.com, Beehiiv waitlist, Prefinery, Viral Loops, Kickofflabs); beta-signal detection ("Beta" badges, "Coming soon", "Early access" CTAs); GitHub `releases.atom` feed for version cadence (when `audit_oss_footprint` resolved an org). Cost ~$0.05. Confidence HIGH for PH+GitHub / MEDIUM for changelog detection.
- **`audit_free_tools(domain, brand, firmographic)` (P40 — Phase 1, unconditional)** — Subdomain enumeration via `crtsh.py` provider (Certificate Transparency logs, free) — filters for tool-pattern subdomains (`tools.`, `app.`, `widgets.`, `calculator.`, `free.`, `labs.`); path probes (`/tools/*`, `/calculators/*`, `/generators/*`, `/free/*`, `/widgets/*`, `/templates/*`, `/checker/*`, `/grader/*`, `/audit/*`); browser extensions via Firefox AMO (`amo.py` provider) + Chrome Web Store (Apify) + Edge Add-ons (DataForSEO `serp_site_query`); SEO-driven tool pages via DataForSEO Labs Keywords-for-Site filtered for `^free|calculator|generator|tool|template|checker` patterns; GitHub repos categorized as standalone tools via `github.py` provider. Classify each hit as "interactive_tool" vs "marketing_page" via DOM heuristic. Cost ~$0.10. Confidence HIGH for subdomain/path/AMO / MEDIUM for Chrome/Edge attribution.
- **`audit_oss_footprint(domain, brand, firmographic)` (P41 — Phase 2, conditional dev-tool/tech firmographic)** — Triggers when `tech_stack` shows API gateway/SDK in stack OR docs subdomain detected OR pricing page mentions "API calls"/"requests"/"tokens" OR firmographic `category="developer_tools"`. Org discovery: domain footer "github.com/X" → homepage `<a href>` → DataForSEO SERP `site:github.com "<brand>"` confirmation. Then via `github.py` GraphQL: org overview + top-5 repos by stars + per-repo (license, contributors-90d, last-commit, README quality, has good-first-issues), CLA detection (CONTRIBUTING.md mentions of CLA + cla-assistant.io), sponsor program (GitHub Sponsors / Open Collective / Polar.sh), contributor employment affiliation (best-effort — GitHub `company` field is freeform). License posture (permissive / copyleft / source-available / mixed). **Cross-link to GEO lens**: high-star repos heavily indexed by Claude/ChatGPT/Perplexity → directly feeds AI-citation supply score. Cost ~$0 (GitHub free at this volume). Confidence HIGH when org found.
- **`audit_customer_education(domain, brand, tech_stack_result)` (P42 — Phase 1, unconditional)** — Path probes (`/academy`, `/university`, `/certifications`, `/learn`, `/training`, `/tutorials`, `/courses`, `/bootcamp`, `/playbook`, `/edu`, `/school`, `/masterclass`); subdomain probes via dnspython CNAME (academy./university./learn./training./edu./courses.); LMS fingerprints via Wappalyzer `lms` category extension (Thinkific `cdn.thinkific.com`, Teachable `data-teachable-app`, Skilljar `skilljarTracker`, Northpass/Gainsight CX, Disco, Docebo `*.docebosaas.com`, LearnUpon, Litmos, Mighty Networks, self-hosted: WordPress LearnDash `/wp-content/plugins/sfwd-lms/`, TalentLMS, Moodle); course count from sitemap (`/course/`, `/lesson/`, `/module/`); certification signals (Credly `credly.com/embed`, Accredible); free-vs-paid (Stripe/Chargebee checkout iframes). Self-hosted LMS = false-negative risk → mitigate with course-card DOM heuristics + Sonnet "is this a course catalog?" classifier on academy-page screenshot. Cost ~$0.00–0.02. Confidence HIGH for vendor-hosted / MEDIUM for self-hosted.
- **`audit_public_roadmap(domain)` (P43 — Phase 1, unconditional)** — Subdomain CNAME probes (`*.canny.io`, `share.productboard.com/<id>/board/`, `*.featurebase.app`, `*.frill.co`, `*.uservoice.com`, `*.productlift.dev`, `*.sleekplan.com`, `*.upvoty.com`, `*.fider.io`, `*.nolt.io`); path probes (`/roadmap`, `/changelog`, `/feedback`, `/feature-requests`, `/ideas`, `/whats-new`, `/public-roadmap`); JS widget fingerprints (Canny `canny.io/sdk.js`, Featurebase `do.featurebase.app/js/sdk.js`, Frill `widget.frill.co`); GitHub Discussions detection; vote-count visibility via DOM regex; status labels ("Planned", "In Progress", "Shipped", "Under Review"); response-rate proxy via "Admin response" / "Team replied" / "Status changed" markers. Cost ~$0.00–0.01. Confidence HIGH for vendor-hosted / MEDIUM for transparency score.
- **`audit_corporate_responsibility(domain, brand, firmographic, serpapi_client)` (P44 — Phase 1, conditional `firmographic.size_band ∈ ["mid_market","enterprise"]`)** — Gated to mid-market+ to avoid 80% false-negative rate on small companies that simply don't publish ESG. Else `{trigger_skipped: true, reason: "size_band_below_threshold"}`. Signals: path probes (`/sustainability`, `/esg`, `/impact`, `/responsibility`, `/csr`, `/diversity`, `/dei`, `/inclusion`, `/accessibility`, `/giving-back`); footer-link keyword detection; PDF discovery via SerpAPI (`site:<domain> filetype:pdf "ESG report"` + variants × 4 keywords); B-Corp directory check (HTTP GET `bcorporation.net/en-us/find-a-b-corp/company/<slug>/` + Apify B-Corp scraper fallback); carbon-neutral/net-zero claims regex on homepage+about; accessibility-statement detection; supplier-diversity / "Pledge 1%" / Benevity widget. Bonus: `gather_voc.NewsDataAdapter` query for "<brand> ESG" / "<brand> sustainability" validates whether claims are press-validated vs unilateral. Cost ~$0.05–0.10. Confidence MEDIUM (high on binary presence, low on quality scoring).
- **`audit_customer_story_program(domain, rendered_fetcher, sonnet_client)` (P45 — Phase 1, unconditional)** — Path probes (`/customers`, `/case-studies`, `/case-study`, `/success`, `/success-stories`, `/stories`, `/customer-stories`, `/clients`, `/use-cases`, `/spotlight`); sitemap-based count via URL-pattern match; cadence via JSON-LD `datePublished` / `<time>` / OpenGraph `article:published_time`; outcome-quantification quality (Sonnet classifier batched 10-per-call: "hard outcomes" via `\d+%`, `\$[\d,]+`, `\d+x`, `\d+\s*(hours?|days?|weeks?|months?)` regex vs "soft outcomes" adjectives only — score = ratio); video presence (`<video>`, youtube/vimeo/wistia embeds); logo-wall vs full case-studies (linked-out vs un-linked logos); customer-led content / UGC detection; G2 + Capterra integration (extend reviews.py with G2 + Capterra Apify scrapers); NPS-quote integration (Delighted, Wootric, AskNicely). Cost ~$0.10–0.30. Confidence HIGH for count/format/cadence / MEDIUM for outcome quality.
- **`audit_trust_signals(rendered_pages, martech_fingerprint, domain)` (P46 — Phase 1, unconditional)** — Trust badge detection (TrustedSite/McAfee Secure `trustedsite.com/services/sealdisplay/v1`, Norton `digicert.com/.../seal/seal.js`, BBB `bbb.org/dynamicseal`, TrustArc); CMP deployment-quality layer over existing `fingerprint_martech_stack` consent category (geo-gated banner detection, Consent Mode v2 wired); security certifications via text mining `/security`, `/trust`, `/compliance`, `/legal` for `\b(SOC\s?2|ISO[- ]?27001|HIPAA|PCI[- ]?DSS|FedRAMP|GDPR|CCPA|FERPA|StateRAMP)\b`; social-proof density (hero customer-logo count via `[class*="logo"]|[class*="customer"]|[class*="trusted-by"]`, footer logo wall, testimonial blocks, review-platform widget integration Trustpilot/G2/Capterra/Yotpo/Bazaarvoice); guarantee/refund language regex `\b(money[- ]back|risk[- ]free|satisfaction guarantee|\d+[- ]day (?:free )?(?:trial|guarantee|refund)|cancel anytime)\b`; security headers via Mozilla HTTP Observatory v2 (replaces SecurityHeaders.com sunsetting April 2026). Cost ~$0.00. Confidence HIGH (deterministic regex + DOM + free Mozilla API).
- **`audit_funnel_content_shape(pages_cache, rendered_homepage, rendered_pricing, firmographic)` (P47 — Phase 3, unconditional, severity-cap=low)** — **Renamed from `audit_funnel_velocity_proxies`** per 2026-04-22 research validation: external signals can describe content/CTA shape but cannot honestly support velocity claims. **Strictly descriptive**, severity ceiling locked at `low`, every finding carries `_caveat: "Descriptive content/CTA shape — not a conversion-quality measure. True funnel velocity requires R20 ad-platform / R25 CRM enrichment."` Signals: TOFU/MOFU/BOFU classification via 1 Sonnet call on 50 sample blog URLs from `analyze_internal_links` corpus; CTA placement audit on homepage + pricing + product + top blog (categorize by verb: demo / trial / buy / content; output dominant pattern per page); gated-vs-ungated content ratio on `/resources/*` URLs; first-case-study date proxy (`founding_year` vs first case-study `datePublished` — flag `confidence: low` since case studies often republished). Cost ~$0.05–0.10. Confidence MEDIUM after reframe (would have been LOW under original velocity framing).
- **`audit_abm_signals(martech_stack, foreplay_ads, sitemap, rendered_fetcher, firmographic)` (P48 — Phase 2, conditional B2B-enterprise)** — Triggers when `firmographic.b2b_enterprise == True` (one or more of: `employee_count >= 500`, has_sales_team_signals, pricing_page="contact_sales", named_industry_verticals_in_nav). Else `{skipped: true, reason: "not_b2b_enterprise"}` — keeps audit honest by avoiding ABM-spam-findings on consumer/SMB prospects. Detection consumes extended `fingerprint_martech_stack` ABM categories (added to `martech_rules.yaml`): **personalization** (Mutiny `client-registry.mutinycdn.com`, RightMessage `widget.rightmessage.com`, Demandbase `tag.demandbase.com` + `*.company-target.com`, 6sense `j.6sc.co/6si.min.js` + `window._6si`, Webeyez, PathFactory, Folloze); **reverse_ip** (Clearbit Reveal `js.clearbit.com/v1/<key>/clearbit.js`, Snitcher, Leadfeeder/Dealfront `sc.lfeeder.com/lftracker_v1`, RB2B `s3-us-west-2.amazonaws.com/b2bjsstore/b/<id>/reb2b.js.gz`, Albacross `serve.albacross.com/track.js` + `window._nQc`, Lead Forensics, Vector, Warmly, Koala); **intent_data** (Bombora text mention + reciprocal backlink, G2 Buyer Intent badge `partnerhub.g2.com/integrations`, ZoomInfo Intent, TechTarget Priority Engine, Gartner Digital Markets); **named-account landing pages** via sitemap URL pattern `^/for/[^/]+/?$|^/industries/[^/]+/?$|^/solutions/[^/]+/?$|^/teams/[^/]+/?$` + simhash similarity across `/for/*` HTML for templated detection (>0.9 = systematic programmatic ABM); **LinkedIn account-targeting** via existing Foreplay LinkedIn ad coverage (seniority/industry signals in ad copy). Output: `abm_maturity_tier ∈ {none, basic, growing, enterprise}` + per-vendor confidence + tool-overlap-bloat flags. Cost ~$0 when triggered (free-tier classification from owned providers). Confidence HIGH for vendor detection / MEDIUM for maturity tier.
- **`audit_plg_motion(rendered_pricing, rendered_signup, rendered_onboarding, firmographic, serpapi_client, sonnet_client)` (Phase 2, conditional SaaS)** — Pricing-page text classification (free trial vs free forever vs freemium vs free plan + trial-length integer + credit-card-required wording); CTA inventory across `/`, `/pricing`, `/product` (self-serve "Start free"/"Get started" vs gated "Talk to sales"/"Book a demo"); form-gating depth (signup field count + SSO buttons); time-to-value advertised on `/getting-started`/`/onboarding`/`/quickstart`; viral mechanisms: (a) "Powered by <brand>" via SerpAPI single query (filter to non-payment-infra brands), (b) public profile pattern `<brand>.com/u/<handle>`, (c) share-to-unlock detection, (d) `/referral`, `/refer-a-friend`, `/affiliates` route presence; **reverse-trial detection** (Verna/OpenView pattern — pricing page mentions both "free plan" AND time-limited "Pro trial"); single Sonnet call synthesizes `motion_type ∈ {pure_freemium, free_trial, reverse_trial, free_tier_forever, gated_demo, hybrid}`. Benchmark output against SaaS conversion rates (freemium ~7%, trial 10–25%; activation freemium 20% vs trial 40%) with directional caveat. Cost ~$0.05. Confidence HIGH.
- **`audit_devex(rendered_docs, github_org, firmographic, sonnet_client)` (Phase 2, conditional dev-tool)** — Triggers when `tech_stack` shows API gateway/SDK OR `/docs`/`/api`/`developer.<domain>` subdomain OR pricing mentions "API calls"/"requests"/"tokens". Docs-platform fingerprint (Mintlify `<meta name="generator" content="Mintlify">`, Stoplight, Redoc `redoc-static.js`, Swagger UI, GitBook, Docusaurus, ReadMe, Scalar — **modern tier vs legacy tier** classification); OpenAPI spec discoverability via parallel HEAD probes (`/openapi.json`, `/openapi.yaml`, `/swagger.json`, `/api/swagger.json`, `/.well-known/openapi`, `/api-docs`, `/api/v1/openapi.json`); quickstart-time signal (word count + code-block count on `/getting-started`); SDK coverage via `github.py` provider (org repos matching `^(<brand>-)?(sdk|client)-(js|ts|python|go|ruby|java|kotlin|swift|php|rust|dotnet)$`); sample apps (`examples?`/`samples?`/`quickstart`/`cookbook` repos); changelog cadence; **SDK version freshness** via npm registry (`registry.npmjs.org/<pkg>/latest` returns `time.modified`) + PyPI JSON (`pypi.org/pypi/<pkg>/json` returns `releases[ver][0].upload_time`) — flag SDKs >180 days since publish; 1 Sonnet call ranks docs quality 0-100 by reading top 3 docs pages (navigation depth, code-sample density, error-message coverage, auth section presence). Cost ~$0.04 (all free APIs + 1 Sonnet quality call). Confidence HIGH.

**2026-04-22 R2 expansion — per-primitive specs (compact; full dossier in `2026-04-22-003-audit-coverage-research-r2.md`):**

*SEO + GEO + Compliance (Group A — 7 net-new primitives + 5 deepening extensions):*

- **`audit_eeat_signals(pages_cache, sonnet_client)` (P49 — Phase 3, unconditional, SEO + GEO)** — Author bios on blog posts, `Person` JSON-LD schema (count, unique authors, `jobTitle`/`worksFor`/`alumniOf`/`sameAs`), visible byline detection, dedicated author archive page (`/author/<slug>/`, `/team/<slug>/`, `/contributors/<slug>/`), credential disclosure regex `\b(MD|PhD|JD|CFA|CPA|CFP|RN|DDS|Esq\.?|MBA)\b` + "Reviewed by" / "Medically reviewed" / "Fact-checked by" sentinel phrases, `/about`, `/editorial-policy`, `/methodology`, `/corrections-policy` page presence, citation density to `.gov`/`.edu`/peer-reviewed sources, "Last updated" / "Reviewed on" date stamps, YMYL classifier (Sonnet, 1 call). **Google's #1 content ranking factor since 2023**; cross-link to GEO (author entities improve AI citation likelihood). Reuses 200-page `analyze_internal_links` corpus. Cost ~$0.03. Confidence HIGH.
- **`audit_robots_strategic(domain)` (P50 — Phase 1, unconditional, SEO + GEO)** — robots.txt fetch + parse + AI crawler controls: GPTBot, ClaudeBot, anthropic-ai, CCBot, Bytespider, Google-Extended, PerplexityBot, OAI-SearchBot, Applebot-Extended, FacebookBot, DiffbotBot allow vs block patterns (maintained list in `src/audit/data/ai_crawler_user_agents.yaml`); standard audit (sitemap declarations, crawl-delay, parameter handling); `meta name="robots" content="noai"` / `noimageai` detection (non-standard but emerging); strategic GEO interpretation (blocking AI crawlers = giving up future AI-search citations vs allowing = increasing AI citation supply). Cost ~$0.00 (free fetch). Confidence HIGH.
- **`audit_crawl_budget_bloat(domain, sitemap_urls)` (P51 — Phase 2, unconditional, SEO)** — Index-bloat detection beyond orphan pages: `?utm=*` indexed variants, faceted-nav URL explosion, paginated archive series (`/page/2/`, `/page/3/`...), parameterized search results in index, near-duplicate URLs from pagination, session-ID URLs. ~20 DataForSEO `site:` queries detecting URL-pattern clusters. Cost ~$0.04. Confidence MEDIUM (cluster classification reliable, absolute counts approximate).
- **`audit_conversational_query_optimization(detect_schema_result, serp_features_result)` (P52 — Phase 3, unconditional, SEO + GEO)** — Composite synthesis on already-collected signals: FAQPage schema + `<h2>`/`<h3>` question-format pattern detection + long-tail conversational keyword targeting + `HowTo`/`QAPage` schema presence + content depth on question pages + AI Overview citation cross-reference. **Renamed from voice-search** since AI search subsumed voice-search era. Reuses `detect_schema` + `analyze_serp_features.people_also_ask`. Cost ~$0.00. Confidence HIGH.
- **`audit_vertical_compliance(domain, firmographic, serpapi_client, sonnet_client)` (P53 — Phase 1, conditional vertical, MarTech-Attribution + Brand/Narrative)** — Per-vertical compliance signal detection per `src/audit/data/vertical_compliance_rules.yaml`: HIPAA BAA availability + HITECH (healthtech), PCI-DSS Level + state MTL/Money Transmitter License (fintech), FERPA + state student-privacy laws (edtech), FDA 510(k) + "Not FDA-evaluated" disclaimers (medical devices), DSA/DMA disclosures (EU large platforms — annual transparency report mandate), SOX (public companies), GLBA (financial services). Path probes + text mining `/security`, `/compliance`, `/trust`, `/legal` + Sonnet completeness pass per vertical. Else `{trigger_skipped: true}`. Cost ~$0.05 when triggered. Confidence MEDIUM (claim detection HIGH; absence ambiguous — could be hidden behind sales gate; frame as "external transparency posture").
- **`audit_ai_policy(domain, rendered_fetcher, sonnet_client)` (P54 — Phase 1, unconditional, Brand/Narrative + MarTech-Attribution)** — Path probes for `/ai-policy`, `/responsible-ai`, `/ai-ethics`, `/ai-governance`, `/ai-principles`; model-training opt-out disclosure detection; AI data usage disclosure; emerging signal increasingly required for Fortune 500 enterprise procurement 2026 (parallel to ESG already in `audit_corporate_responsibility`). 1 Sonnet quality pass on detected pages. Cost ~$0.03. Confidence HIGH (presence) / MEDIUM (substantive evaluation).
- **`audit_sustainability_carbon(domain, pagespeed_data)` (P55 — Phase 2 sub of `audit_corporate_responsibility`, unconditional, Brand/Narrative)** — Free Website Carbon Calculator API (`https://api.websitecarbon.com/site?url=<url>`) + Green Web Foundation greencheck (`https://api.thegreenwebfoundation.org/api/v3/greencheck/<domain>`) + page-weight from existing PageSpeed data + sustainability commitment-page parsing (Sonnet pass). Cost ~$0.01. Confidence MEDIUM (CO2 estimate order-of-magnitude only; green-hosting check HIGH; commitment page boolean signals HIGH).
- **Footer optimization** (extends `audit_on_page_seo`) — Footer link distribution density + NAP citation cross-check with `audit_local_seo` + trust badges in footer + social-proof in footer. Parses already-fetched homepage. Cost ~$0.00. Confidence HIGH (struct) / MEDIUM (badge ID).
- **Documentation translations** (extends `audit_help_center_docs`, conditional dev-tool) — Multilingual docs depth: Mintlify `docs.json` config inspection + Docusaurus URL pattern (`/docs/<lang>/`) + GitBook multi-language config + hreflang on docs subdomain + language switcher widget detection. Cost ~$0.00. Confidence HIGH (Mintlify/Docusaurus) / MEDIUM (GitBook + custom).
- **Sub-processor / DPA disclosure** (extends `audit_trust_signals`) — Path probes `/legal/sub-processors`, `/dpa`, `/data-processing` + completeness scoring (sub-processor list, data-residency disclosure, retention policy, transfer mechanisms, change-notification process) via Sonnet pass when found. **Required for B2B EU enterprise sales (Art. 28 GDPR).** Cost ~$0.02. Confidence HIGH (presence) / MEDIUM (completeness).
- **Backlink anchor-text branded-vs-commercial breakdown** (extends `analyze_backlinks`) — Classify each backlink anchor-text as branded / commercial / naked-URL / generic ("click here", "read more") / branded-keyword mix. Compute distribution + flag over-optimization (>30% commercial = penalty risk). Anchor data already in `analyze_backlinks` payload — pure synthesis. Cost ~$0.00. Confidence HIGH (dist) / MEDIUM (risk threshold interpretation).
- **`audit_schema_competitive(detect_schema_prospect, scan_competitor_pages_result)` (Reasoning, unconditional, SEO synthesis)** — Pure synthesis comparing prospect schema coverage to top 3 competitors detected by `scan_competitor_pages`. Output: per-schema-type presence delta ("competitors all use FAQPage + HowTo; you only have Organization"). Deterministic logic on existing data. Cost ~$0.00. Confidence HIGH.

*Brand + Narrative + PR (Group B — 4 net-new primitives + 9 deepening extensions; diversity-imagery REJECTED by research due to LOW confidence + litigation risk):*

- **`audit_branded_serp(brand, dataforseo_client)` (P56 — Phase 1, unconditional, Brand/Narrative)** — DataForSEO SERP Advanced (`/v3/serp/google/organic/live/advanced`) for 4 brand-name queries (`<brand>`, `<brand> reviews`, `<brand> alternatives`, `<brand> pricing`); single call returns Knowledge Panel + sitelinks + reviews stars + AI Overview cited sources + PAA defensive queries (`is X legit?`, `is X scam?`, `is X safe?`, `is X down?`) + top stories + featured snippet. Compute "owned real estate" count (organic top-10 belonging to brand domain + owned subdomains + owned social handles). Cost $0.003 (4 queries × $0.0006). Confidence HIGH.
- **`audit_branded_autosuggest(brand)` (P57 — Phase 1, unconditional, Brand/Narrative + Monitoring)** — Google autosuggest endpoint `http://suggestqueries.google.com/complete/search?client=chrome&q=<seed>` for 10 seeds (`<brand>`, `<brand> is`, `<brand> review`, `<brand> alternatives`, `<brand> vs`, `<brand> down`, `<brand> pricing`, `<brand> login`, `<brand> safe`, `<brand> scam`); compute distribution of defensive vs neutral vs commercial autosuggest. SerpAPI fallback if rate-limited. Cost ~$0.00 (free) / $0.05 worst-case. Confidence HIGH.
- **`audit_industry_analyst_position(brand, firmographic, serpapi_client, rendered_fetcher)` (P58 — Phase 2, unconditional, Brand/Narrative + Competitive)** — **Single largest remaining B2B SaaS finding.** SerpAPI brand-name + analyst-firm queries (`"<brand>" "magic quadrant"`, `"<brand>" "forrester wave"`, `"<brand>" "g2 leader"`, `"<brand>" "capterra shortlist"`, `"<brand>" "idc marketscape"`); scrape brand's own marketing pages declaring "Gartner MQ Leader 2024" (self-promoted analyst position is HIGH-confidence signal); cached awards lookup from `analyst_position_awards.yaml` (Inc 5000 / Fast Company Most Innovative / Deloitte Fast 500 / Comparably awards / Built In awards); G2 Grid quadrant scrape attempt (Cloudflare-blocked — accept partial). **Gartner MQ "Leader" alone drives 30-50% of enterprise close rate.** Cost ~$0.01. Confidence HIGH (self-promoted via marketing pages + SERP triangulation) / MEDIUM (G2 quadrant detail) / LOW (direct Gartner/Forrester reports paywalled — accept this).
- **`audit_clv_retention_signals(brand, domain, serpapi_client, news_adapter)` (P59 — Phase 2, unconditional, Brand/Narrative + Conversion)** — Public NPS publication (`"<brand>" "NPS" OR "Net Promoter"`), customer-retention rate claims ("99.7% of customers stay"), expansion-revenue case study signals, GRR/NRR mentions (via NewsData + Wayback shareholder-letter snapshots), customer-base growth charts. 6 SERP queries + 1 news + Wayback CDX + 1 Sonnet extraction. Cost ~$0.03. Confidence MEDIUM-HIGH (signal density low for private cos; most utility for series-B+ SaaS).
- **Newsletter quality** (extends `audit_content_strategy_shape` newsletter sub) — Beyond subscriber-count claim: cadence consistency (last-N issues date analysis), open-graph card quality on newsletter posts, archive depth, recent-issue Sonnet quality pass on 2-3 issues for prose quality + signal-to-promo ratio. Cost ~$0.06.
- **Newsletter leaderboard rank** (extends `audit_content_strategy_shape` newsletter sub) — Substack `/discover/rising` + `/discover/top` per category + Beehiiv `/explore` + ConvertKit `kit.com/<handle>` + SparkLoop network indicator. Cost ~$0.05 (only fires when newsletter detected → rare).
- **Original research depth** (extends `audit_content_strategy_shape`) — PR coverage of research via DataForSEO Backlinks anchor-text matching report titles + 5 reports × refresh-cadence detection + 1 Sonnet methodology-disclosure pass. Cost ~$0.13.
- **Owned podcast quality** (extends `audit_podcast_footprint`, conditional owned-podcast detected) — Cadence consistency + Podchaser ratings/reviews + guest-tier (recurring big-name guests vs unknown — cross-reference firmographic-vertical executive list) + production-quality proxies (transcript availability via Pod Engine, show-notes depth). Cost ~$0.02.
- **Wire-service vs original-pitch press ratio** (extends `audit_earned_media_footprint`) — Cision / PRNewswire / Business Wire / GlobeNewswire / Newsfile boilerplate-language detection in press releases (host classification deterministic + Sonnet body-pass). Wire-only press = press-release-machine pattern; original-pitch = real PR rigor. Cost ~$0.02–0.05.
- **M&A history** (extends `audit_earned_media_footprint`) — 5 NewsData queries (`"<brand>" acquisition OR "acquired by" OR merger OR "merged with"`) + 2 SERP + Wikipedia + Sonnet extraction. Cost ~$0.03.
- **Brand demand trend** (extends `gather_voc`) — `GoogleTrendsAdapter` (already owned) on brand-name + `<brand> reviews` + `<brand> pricing`. **Cleanest top-of-funnel demand signal.** Compute trajectory (growing/flat/declining), seasonality, breakout-related-queries. Cost ~$0.14.
- **Comments engagement on owned content** (extends `audit_partnership_event_community_footprint`) — Disqus / Hyvor Talk / Commento / Cusdis / Remark42 detection + native CMS comments + Reddit megathread cross-ref via existing Xpoz adapter + exec-response patterns (heuristic: comment author matches firmographic exec roster). Cost ~$0.02.
- **Rebrand history Wayback** (extends `audit_messaging_consistency`) — Logo evolution via pHash diff on Wayback historical hero images + name-change via meta-title diff + domain-migration via Wayback redirects history + 1 Sonnet tagline-drift pass. Reuses existing Wayback usage. Cost ~$0.02.
- **Brand voice cross-platform analysis** (extends `audit_messaging_consistency` voice-consistency sub) — Distinct from positioning consistency: Twitter/X account voice (formality, humor, jargon density) vs LinkedIn vs blog vs founder personal-X voice. Reuse adapter calls + spaCy/textstat (free) + 1 Sonnet batched cross-surface voice pass. Cost ~$0.05.

*Conversion + Trust + Funnel + Sales (Group C — 9 net-new primitives + 3 deepening extensions):*

- **`audit_customer_support(rendered_fetcher, martech_stack_result, sonnet_client)` (P60 — Phase 2, unconditional, Conversion + Lifecycle)** — Live chat widget detection (Intercom `widget.intercom.io/widget/<APP_ID>`, Drift `js.driftt.com`, Crisp `client.crisp.chat/l.js`, Tidio `code.tidio.co`, Tawk.to, LiveChat, Zendesk, Olark, HubSpot Chat — already in `fingerprint_martech_stack`); deployment quality via 2× Playwright (open-hours + after-hours simulation): office hours visible, multilingual support detection (greeting language switcher), bot-vs-human triage UX, response-time SLA published, AI chatbot quality (on-brand, escalation-to-human path), support-language coverage. Cost ~$0.03–0.06. Confidence HIGH (vendor + business hours) / MEDIUM (after-hours + bot-vs-human).
- **`audit_cro_experimentation_maturity(rendered_fetcher, martech_stack_result)` (P61 — Phase 1, unconditional, Conversion)** — Beyond vendor presence (Optimizely / VWO / Convert / AB Tasty / Statsig / GrowthBook / Eppo / Split.io detected): cookie-pattern detection (`_optly_*`, `_vwo_uuid`, `_ab`, `cv_*`); URL parameters (`?vid=`, `?test=`, `?variant=`); Wayback diffs of pricing/CTA copy showing variant rotation last 12 months. Cost ~$0.02. Confidence HIGH (vendor + cookie) / MEDIUM (cadence inference) / LOW (server-side blind spot).
- **`audit_ecommerce_catalog(rendered_fetcher, firmographic, sonnet_client)` (P62 — Phase 2, conditional DTC/e-comm firmographic, Conversion)** — Per-SKU image count + structured `Product` schema + `AggregateRating` schema + customer review density per SKU + recommendations engine detection (Klaviyo Reviews, Yotpo, Bazaarvoice, Searchspring, Algolia Recommend, Constructor, Bloomreach) + guest-checkout option + checkout flow step count + faceted search/sort UX. E-commerce platform detection (Shopify/BigCommerce/WooCommerce/Magento/SFCC). Cost ~$0.05–0.15 depending on PDP-sample size. Confidence HIGH (platform/schema/reviews vendor) / MEDIUM (review density SSR variance) / LOW (checkout flow shape — needs R23).
- **`audit_b2c_personalization(martech_stack_result, firmographic)` (P63 — Phase 1, conditional B2C/DTC firmographic, Conversion)** — Distinct from `audit_abm_signals` (B2B): Dynamic Yield (`window.DY`), Optimizely Web Personalization, Adobe Target (`window.adobe.target`), VWO Personalize, Insider (`Insider.eventManager`), Bloomreach Engagement (`exponea`), Movable Ink (`mi.js` — primarily email/post-checkout, light on-page JS), Persado, Rokt. JS detection patterns + cookie signatures via extended `martech_rules.yaml` `b2c_personalization` category. Optional geo-variance test (Playwright with `setGeolocation`). Cost ~$0.01 base / $0.06 with geo-variance. Confidence HIGH (vendor) / MEDIUM (active runtime) / LOW (campaign maturity).
- **`audit_homepage_demo_video(rendered_fetcher, youtube_api)` (P64 — Phase 1, unconditional, Conversion)** — Wistia (`fast.wistia.net`), Vimeo, Loom (`loom.com/embed/`), YouTube embed, Mux (`stream.mux.com`), Cloudflare Stream, Bunny Stream. View-count proxies (Wistia public stats, YouTube oEmbed view counts), video chapter markers, transcript availability, captions in multiple languages, CTA-after-video presence, autoplay vs click-to-play, video duration analysis. Distinct from `audit_youtube_channel` (owned channel). Cost ~$0.01. Confidence HIGH (embed/platform/duration/captions) / MEDIUM (view counts YouTube only) / LOW (qualitative score).
- **`audit_first_party_data_strategy(rendered_fetcher, martech_stack_result, sonnet_client)` (P65 — Phase 2, unconditional, MarTech-Attribution + Conversion)** — Quizzes / configurators / surveys for first-party data collection (Typeform, Tally, Outgrow, Riddle, Jotform, Ceros, Octane.ai detection); progressive profiling on forms (multi-step forms with progressive field reveal); CDP integration cross-reference via `fingerprint_martech_stack` CDP category (Segment, RudderStack, Tealium, mParticle); privacy-first marketing posture (zero-party data UX language). 1 Sonnet pass. Cost ~$0.03. Confidence HIGH (vendor/path) / MEDIUM (marketing-vs-in-product classification + progressive profiling).
- **`audit_trust_center(rendered_fetcher, martech_stack_result, dns_resolver, sonnet_client)` (P66 — Phase 1, unconditional, Conversion + MarTech-Attribution)** — Self-serve security review platform detection: SafeBase (`safebase.io` subdomain or `cdn.safebase.io`), Vanta Trust Center (`trust.vanta.com` or `trust.<brand>.com`), Drata Trust Hub (`trust.drata.com`), Whistic, Conveyor, OneTrust Vendorpedia, SecurityScorecard ATLAS, ScrutXray. **Cuts enterprise sales cycle 30-60 days when present.** Cost ~$0.02. Confidence HIGH (vendor/URL + cert inventory) / MEDIUM (self-serve depth qualitative score).
- **`audit_sales_motion_classification(audit_pricing_page_result, scrape_careers_result, capture_surface_scan_result, tech_stack_result, sonnet_client)` (P67 — Phase 3, reasoning-only synthesis, unconditional, Synthesis)** — Composes from existing primitives: pricing-transparency binary (public Y/N from `audit_pricing_page`) + sales-rep LinkedIn enumeration count (from `scrape_careers` + LinkedIn page metadata) + "Talk to Sales" CTA gating depth (from `capture_surface_scan` enterprise_gating_signals) + outbound sales tool detection (Apollo/Outreach/Salesloft/Lemlist/Smartlead via `tech_stack` + JD mentions). Sonnet classifier outputs `motion_type ∈ {plg, inside_sales, enterprise_sales, hybrid_plg_to_sales, hybrid_smb_to_enterprise}`. Major synthesis layer informing engagement-scope conversation. Cost ~$0.02. Confidence HIGH.
- **`audit_mobile_ux(rendered_fetcher_mobile)` (P68 — Phase 1, unconditional, Conversion + SEO)** — One extra Playwright fetch in mobile mode (375×667 viewport): touch target sizes (44×44 px iOS / 48×48 dp Android per HIG/Material), viewport meta validity, mobile checkout flow steps (extends `audit_ecommerce_catalog`), hamburger nav UX quality, mobile-first form patterns (input types `tel`/`email`/`number`, `inputmode` attributes), AMP detection, mobile-specific responsive image handling. - **Push notification opt-in strategy** (extends `capture_surface_scan`) — OneSignal (`onesignal.com/sdks/`), Pushwoosh (`cdn.pushwoosh.com`), Pusher Beams (`js.pusher.com/beams`), VWO Engage, Firebase Cloud Messaging, WonderPush, Iterable web push, PushOwl (Shopify). Per-discussion fields: `id`, `title`, `category {name}`, `createdAt`, `isAnswered`, `answer {author {login}, createdAt}`, `comments(first: 5) {nodes {author {login}, createdAt, authorAssociation}}`. `authorAssociation` enum (`OWNER`/`MEMBER`/`COLLABORATOR`/`CONTRIBUTOR`/`NONE`) → team-vs-community classifier. - **`audit_welcome_email_signup(plg_motion_result, audit_id, opt_in_flag, disposable_email_provider, sonnet_client)` (P84 — Phase 3, conditional free-trial/freemium detected + manual user opt-in flag, PLG + Lifecycle + MarTech)** — Performs throwaway-email signup on detected free trial / freemium / newsletter to inspect welcome email design + sender reputation + CAN-SPAM compliance + transactional-email design quality. Disposable-email provider: Mailinator public inbox (free, world-readable) → Maildrop / GuerrillaMail / tempmail.io fallback; identifiable inbox `gofreddy-audit-{audit_id[:8]}@mailinator.com`. **CRITICAL safety pattern updated 2026-04-22 R4 (CFAA + ToS risk; ~50-60% signup success due to disposable-email blocklists)**: (1) **Capability restriction (primary)** — runs under scoped `ClaudeSDKClient` session with `build_welcome_email_toolbelt()` from `src/audit/scoped_tools.py` exposing only IMAP-read + DNS-lookup + Sonnet-classify + narrow `submit_signup_form(fields)` Playwright wrapper. The wrapper rejects payment-field inputs at the wrapper level (before they reach Playwright); agent cannot invoke `page.click` on email links because the tool isn't exposed. (2) **Orchestrator pre-conditions** in `src/audit/stages.py` before primitive invocation: `if not opt_in_flag: raise OptInRequired`; `if state.welcome_email_completed: raise AlreadyRun` (1-shot cap); `if not identifiable_fixture(email): raise FixtureValidation`. (3) Manual-fire only (NEVER scheduled). (4) Identifiable test fixture name (`Audit GoFreddy-{audit_id}`). (5) Per-form human confirmation — CLI prompts "Agent prepared signup for <domain>. Submit? [y/N]" at form.submit() moment. (6) Honor "uncheck marketing" boxes during signup (wrapper default-unchecks any field matching `marketing|promotional|offers|newsletter` keyword). (7) One-shot inbox discard. (8) Engagement letter disclosure that audit may include single test signup. Captures: latency, sender domain match, sender display name (human-named vs no-reply), DKIM/SPF/DMARC pass, CAN-SPAM compliance (physical address, unsubscribe link), GDPR opt-in language, HTML quality (mobile-responsive, dark-mode, alt-text), CTA count + placement, personalization tokens, **email signature fingerprinting cross-feed to P79**. Cost ~$0.10 / $3.30 amortized at scale with private Mailinator domain ($99/mo). Confidence MEDIUM.
- **`audit_public_company_ir(brand, firmographic, sec_edgar_client, rendered_fetcher, serpapi_client)` (P85 — Phase 1, conditional public-company firmographic, Brand/Narrative)** — IR page presence at standard paths (`/investor-relations`, `/investors`, `/ir`, `investors.<domain>`); SEC EDGAR APIs (free, 10 req/sec, User-Agent header required): ticker → CIK lookup via `company_tickers.json` (~3MB daily-refresh) + filings history via `data.sec.gov/submissions/CIK<10-digit-padded>.json`; latest 10-K, 10-Q, 8-K filing dates; earnings call transcript availability; analyst coverage list; press-release-vs-earnings ratio (last 12mo); proxy statement (DEF 14A); ESG report linkage cross-reference; IR contact dedicated email/phone; stock chart widget (Q4/NIRI-style). US-only (foreign listings need 20-F/6-K). Cost ~$0.02. Confidence HIGH (filings) / MEDIUM (IR-page quality).
- **`audit_hiring_funnel_ux(scrape_careers_result, ats_vendor, rendered_fetcher, sonnet_client)` (P86 — Phase 2, conditional ATS detected, Brand/Narrative + Conversion)** — When ATS detected (Greenhouse/Lever/Ashby/Workable already extracted): application-form structure via ATS public APIs (Greenhouse `?questions=true` returns full questions schema; Ashby Job Posting API; Lever public API only gives high-level posting → fall back to Playwright DOM); field-count audit (required vs optional), field-type distribution, HTML5 autocomplete attributes (reuses `_deep_inspect_forms()` from P23), multi-step vs single-page, mobile-responsive, accessibility (axe-playwright), document-upload UX, demographic-question presence + GDPR consent pattern (Greenhouse `data_compliance` field), salary-range disclosure (state-law compliance for CA/NY/CO/WA), social-apply (LinkedIn/Indeed Apply), time-to-fill heuristic. **Critical safety pattern updated 2026-04-22 R4: capability restriction prevents fraudulent application submission.** Runs under scoped session with `build_hiring_funnel_toolbelt()` — Playwright observation only (`page.goto`, `locator.get_attribute`, `page.accessibility.snapshot`, axe-playwright for a11y) + ATS public-API clients (read-only). NO `page.click`, NO `page.fill`, NO `form.submit()` exposed. Agent physically cannot submit the form because submit isn't in its toolbelt. Render-only DOM inspection via `_deep_inspect_forms()` from P23 provides field-structure analysis. Cost ~$0.03. Confidence HIGH (Greenhouse/Ashby) / MEDIUM (Lever) / MEDIUM-LOW (Workable + custom).

**Files:**
- Create `src/audit/rendered_fetcher.py` — `RenderedFetcher` class (context manager, single shared browser context per audit)
- Create `src/audit/primitives.py` — **R5 2026-04-22**: shrinks to ~2 local-only helpers (`fingerprint_martech_stack` + `content_strategy_embeddings_cluster`). The Phase 1/2/3 listings below served R3+R4 as the dependency graph of ~83 Python functions; under R5 they are preserved as a **coverage-reference catalog** — each entry names a signal/rubric the pre-discovery Sonnet agent or Stage-2 agent must investigate via WebFetch or cache-backed tool (per the prompt-mention pattern described at the top of U2). Dependency ordering is implicit in Stage 1 (cache warmup precedes Sonnet pre-discovery) rather than encoded in a `primitive_registry.yaml`. Phase 1 (independent, no inputs from other primitives): all R1 Phase 1 listings PLUS R2 additions `audit_eeat_signals`, `audit_robots_strategic`, `audit_ai_policy`, `audit_branded_serp`, `audit_branded_autosuggest`, `audit_reddit_ama_brand_subreddit`, `audit_branded_merchandise_swag`, `audit_customer_advisory_board_references` (cond B2B), `audit_university_academic_partnerships` (cond research-heavy/dev-tool/edtech), `audit_geographic_expansion`, `audit_huggingface_presence` (cond AI), `audit_b2c_personalization` (cond B2C/DTC, Phase 1 since martech-stack-only), `audit_homepage_demo_video`, `audit_trust_center`, `audit_mobile_ux`, `audit_email_signature_marketing_indicators`, `audit_error_page_ux`, `audit_public_company_ir` (cond public), `audit_cro_experimentation_maturity`. Phase 2 R1+R2 includes (depend on Phase 1 outputs): all R1 Phase 2 PLUS R2 additions `audit_industry_analyst_position` (depends on firmographic vertical), `audit_clv_retention_signals` (depends on firmographic + news adapter), `audit_customer_support` (depends on `fingerprint_martech_stack` chat vendor detection), `audit_ecommerce_catalog` (cond DTC, depends on platform detection), `audit_first_party_data_strategy` (depends on `fingerprint_martech_stack` CDP category), `audit_crawl_budget_bloat` (depends on sitemap), `audit_vertical_compliance` (depends on firmographic vertical), `audit_mobile_app_linking` (depends on `audit_aso` mobile-app detection), `audit_influencer_ftc_compliance` (depends on existing IC + Xpoz creator content), `audit_hackathon_dev_event_sponsorships` (cond dev-tool), `audit_open_api_public_data_access`, `audit_github_discussions_volume` (depends on `audit_oss_footprint` GitHub Discussions enabled), `audit_sustainability_carbon` (depends on PageSpeed data), `audit_ctv_ads_detection` (depends on Foreplay), `audit_apple_search_ads` (cond mobile + R20), `audit_hiring_funnel_ux` (cond ATS detected). Phase 3 R1+R2 includes (multi-input): all R1 Phase 3 PLUS R2 additions `audit_conversational_query_optimization` (synthesis on `detect_schema` + `analyze_serp_features`), `audit_schema_competitive` (synthesis on `detect_schema` + `scan_competitor_pages`), `audit_sales_motion_classification` (reasoning composing `audit_pricing_page` + `scrape_careers` + `capture_surface_scan` + `tech_stack`), `audit_welcome_email_signup` (cond free-trial + opt-in flag, depends on `audit_plg_motion`), `audit_paywall_upgrade_cro` (cond freemium, depends on `audit_pricing_page`):
  - `tech_stack(rendered_page) -> dict` — python-Wappalyzer + custom regex rules for pixels, server-side tagging, modern auth
  - `enumerate_subdomains(domain) -> dict` — crt.sh HTTP + `subfinder` CLI + `whois` CLI, classify live/parked/404
  - `scrape_careers(domain, firmographic) -> dict` — **extended 2026-04-22** with employer-brand deepening + ATS public APIs as primary path. Try ATS public job-board APIs first (free, reliable): Greenhouse `boards-api.greenhouse.io/v1/boards/<token>/jobs?content=true`, Lever `api.lever.co/v0/postings/<co>?mode=json`, Ashby `api.ashbyhq.com/posting-api/job-board/<co>`, Workable per-company JSON — detects ATS via parallel HEAD probes. Gets open-roles count + roles-by-department + full JD content (extract tech-stack mentions via Sonnet) + **salary-range disclosure per role** for pay-transparency compliance check (CA/NY/CO/WA/IL/MD/HI/MN/RI/VT/MA jurisdictions — CA 15+ employees fines $100-$10K/violation, NY 4+ employees NYC fines up to $250K, CO 1+ employee fines $500-$10K, WA 15+ employees $100-$5K/violation). **Pay-transparency compliance is the publishable anchor finding** ("Acme posts 40 CA roles without salary ranges = $400K legal exposure"). Fallback to `/careers`, `/jobs`, `/work-with-us` page scrape when no ATS detected. **LinkedIn company-page metadata** via Apify `harvestapi/linkedin-company-employees` page-only mode (~$0.05/audit — followers + employee count + growth rate + recent posts; do NOT pull employee enumeration at $4-$8/1K which rate-limits). **Glassdoor via Bright Data** Cloudflare-bypass scraping optional Tier-2 enrichment (~$0.10-0.50/audit, 70-80% success) — escalate only for >$10M revenue prospects. **Comparably** public profile scrape via RenderedFetcher for cultural-dimension breakdowns by gender/ethnicity (free, polite 1 req/2s). **Indeed Company Pages** via RenderedFetcher at low volume OR Apify `epctex/indeed-scraper` at scale — primary survivor of Glassdoor/Indeed July 2025 Recruit Holdings merger. Returns `{ats_platform, open_roles_count, open_roles_by_dept, hiring_velocity (roles÷employees), new_roles_30d, tech_stack_mentions, salary_transparency: {per-jurisdiction compliance %}, pay_transparency_violations[], linkedin_{followers, employees, growth_12mo}, glassdoor_{rating, review_count}|null, comparably_culture_scores|null, indeed_rating|null}`. Conditional Glassdoor escalation logic in implementation
  - `scrape_firmographics(domain) -> dict` — Crunchbase public page + LinkedIn company page via rendered fetcher; Sonnet structured extraction
  - `detect_schema(rendered_page) -> dict` — parse JSON-LD blocks, flag missing high-value types
  - `score_ai_visibility(brand, queries, competitors) -> dict` — wraps existing `src/geo/providers/cloro.py`. Returns `{platform: {response_text_word_count, citation_count, citations: [{url, title, source, position, position_weight, word_pos_score}], sov_vs_competitors, is_cited, avg_cite_position}}`. Exposes Cloro's **positional metrics** (`position_weight`: 1st=1.0, 2nd=0.8, 3rd=0.6, 4th+=0.4; `word_pos_score` = word_count × position_weight) — these let the GEO lens distinguish "cited but always last" from "cited first every time," which is the finding that actually matters. Aggregates: per-platform citation counts, share-of-voice vs competitors on the same prompts, gap analysis
  - `scan_competitor_pages(prospect_domain, competitor_domains) -> dict` — fetch sitemaps, grep `/vs/`, `/alternatives/`, `/compare/`
  - `gather_voc(brand, platforms) -> dict` — parallel fan-out across 10 owned monitoring adapters. Data sources (all owned, see "Data provider inventory"):
    - `XpozAdapter` → Twitter + Instagram + Reddit posts (with engagement, relevance, inauthenticity scores)
    - `ICContentAdapter` (dual-instantiated for TikTok + YouTube) → creator content mentioning the brand
    - `TrustpilotAdapter` + `AppStoreAdapter` + `PlayStoreAdapter` → review corpus (rating, sentiment, business reply, verified flag)
    - `NewsDataAdapter` → press mentions with sentiment + `ai_tags` + `source_priority`
    - `PodEngineAdapter` → podcast transcript matches with `is_ad_segment` flag (filter sponsorships out of true VoC)
    - `BlueskyMentionFetcher` → free Bluesky mentions
    - `FacebookMentionFetcher` + `LinkedInMentionFetcher` → Apify-backed public-post scrapers
    - `GoogleTrendsAdapter` → search-interest trend context + related queries (demand-side VoC signal)

    Returns `{by_source: {<DataSource>: [RawMention]}, aggregated: {pain_points[], praise_themes[], sentiment_distribution, source_tier_breakdown, trend_signals{}}}`. One Sonnet pass synthesizes raw mentions into pain-point/praise clusters. Graceful per-adapter degradation (any subset of adapters returning `partial=true` proceeds). **R5 2026-04-22**: `gather_voc` is no longer a standalone `primitives.py` function — its logic is wrapped by `src/audit/tools/monitoring_tool.py:voc(brand, platforms[])` which dispatches to the 12 existing `src/monitoring/adapters/*.py` adapters with internal `Semaphore(10)` fan-out. Stage 1 warmup invokes it unconditionally for owned-monitoring signal priming; Stage 2 agents (Monitoring, Distribution, Brand/Narrative) call it at runtime for cache-hit reads + drill-down fetches
  - `detect_analytics_tags(rendered_page) -> dict` — **DEPRECATED, superseded by `fingerprint_martech_stack` (primitive 25).** Retained as a thin shim that calls `fingerprint_martech_stack` and returns only the analytics-tag subset for backward-compat during migration. Delete once `fingerprint_martech_stack` is shipped.
  - **`analyze_backlinks(domain) -> dict`** — DataForSEO Backlinks API. Prospect-domain-only in Stage 1. Returns `{total_backlinks, referring_domains, dataforseo_rank, new_lost_30d, top_referring_domains[{domain, rank, links_count, category}], anchor_text_distribution, toxic_signals}`. The `dataforseo_rank` field is DataForSEO's proprietary authority score (0–1000 scale) — it is NOT equivalent to Moz DA or Ahrefs DR and the deliverable names it explicitly to avoid confusion. Feeds SEO lens (prospect's linking health); head-to-head competitor backlink comparison runs inside the **U4 competitive lens in Stage 2**, after `derive_competitors` has resolved the final competitor list (see U4 Approach). Graceful degradation if API rate-limited → `partial=true` with subset data.
  - **`audit_page_speed(urls) -> dict`** — Google PageSpeed Insights API (free, 25K queries/day). Called for up to ~10 key URLs (homepage, top 3 landing pages from sitemap, pricing, top blog post). Internally calls both `mobile` and `desktop` strategies per URL — callers get both in one return. Return shape: `{url: {mobile: {performance_score, lcp, inp, cls, opportunities[], diagnostics[]}, desktop: {...same shape...}}}`. Feeds SEO lens (Core Web Vitals is a Google ranking factor) + conversion lens (page speed directly affects bounce rate). Per-URL failures stay partial without failing the whole primitive.
  - **`historical_rank_trends(domain, keywords, timeframe="6mo") -> dict`** — DataForSEO Labs `Historical Search Volume` endpoint (keyword demand trend) + `Historical Rank Overview` endpoint (prospect's rank trajectory over time). Returns `{organic_traffic_trend: [{month, sessions_est}], keyword_rank_history[{keyword, rank_series[{date, rank}]}], visibility_index_series[{date, index}], notable_drops[{keyword, from_rank, to_rank, date}], notable_gains[same shape]}`. Feeds SEO lens (trend context turns a static finding into "declining for 6 months — urgent") + synthesis (historical context enables better "surprises"). Fallback: if no historical data available (brand-new domain), returns `{partial: true, missing_fields: ["historical"]}` and lenses proceed with snapshot-only signals.
  - **`keyword_gap_analysis(domain) -> dict`** — DataForSEO Labs `Competitors Keywords` + `Domain Intersection` endpoints. Auto-discovers top 20–50 SERP competitors by keyword overlap (independent of form-provided competitor list — that list seeds other primitives; this one surfaces whoever is actually competing for the prospect's keyword space). Returns `{prospect_keywords_count, top_competitors_by_overlap[{domain, overlap_count, missing_from_prospect_count, avg_rank}], keyword_gaps[{keyword, search_volume, competitor_rank, competitor_domain, opportunity_score}]` (top 100 gaps ranked by opportunity score = volume × ease × commercial intent)`}`. Feeds SEO lens (the biggest quick-win inventory SaaS users expect) + competitive lens (SERP-competitor picture). Graceful degradation on API quota exhaustion → returns top 25 gaps with `partial=true`.
  - **`analyze_serp_features(keywords) -> dict`** — DataForSEO SERP API. For up to 30 prospect-relevant keywords (drawn from `historical_rank_trends` + `keyword_gap_analysis` output — not independently picked, so this primitive runs AFTER those two), returns per-keyword SERP feature inventory: `{keyword: {featured_snippet: {present, owner_domain, opportunity_score}, people_also_ask[{question, answer_owner}], knowledge_panel: {present, entity}, ai_overview: {present, cited_domains[]}, related_searches[], video_carousel[], shopping_results[], image_pack}, ...}`. Feeds SEO lens (featured-snippet capture opportunities is a top SaaS insight) + GEO lens (`ai_overview.cited_domains` is the strongest public signal of AI-search citation, complementing `score_ai_visibility`). Graceful degradation on per-keyword failure leaves that keyword marked `partial`.
  - **`analyze_internal_links(domain, sitemap_urls) -> dict`** — Internal link-graph analysis (Screaming Frog / Sitebulb parity). Consumes sitemap output (already produced by `freddy sitemap` subprocess). Fetches up to 200 pages via `httpx` (not Playwright — link extraction doesn't need JS rendering; static HTML + BeautifulSoup is faster and cheaper); for sites under 200 pages, does a full crawl. **The 200-page HTML corpus this primitive fetches is shared with `audit_on_page_seo` and `audit_content_quality` (both below) — fetch-once, parse-three-times — to avoid 3× HTTP cost.** Extracts `<a href>` tags, builds an internal link graph, computes depth from homepage. Returns `{page_count_crawled, crawl_coverage_pct, orphan_pages[{url, has_canonical, indexable}], deep_pages[{url, min_clicks_from_home}] (threshold: >3 clicks), broken_internal_links[{from_url, to_url, status_code}], link_equity_distribution: {top_linked_pages[{url, incoming_links}], tail_pages_pct}, anchor_text_internal_distribution, _raw_pages_cache}`. Feeds SEO lens (orphans and deep pages are common fixable wins that are visible in Screaming Frog but not in SEMrush/Ahrefs by default). Graceful degradation: large sites exceeding 200 pages → `partial=true` with sample; crawler blocked by robots.txt → `partial=true` with what was reached; total crawl cap 10 min to bound wall-clock.
  - **`audit_on_page_seo(pages_cache) -> dict`** — Per-URL technical SEO audit (Screaming Frog page-level parity). Consumes the 200-page HTML corpus already fetched by `analyze_internal_links` (no new HTTP). Parses each page for: `{url: {title: {text, length, is_duplicate_across_site}, meta_description: {text, length, is_duplicate}, h1: {count, text}, heading_hierarchy: {h1_count, h2_count, ..., issues[]} (flags skipped levels), canonical: {url, is_self, is_cross_domain}, directives: {noindex, nofollow, noarchive}, images: {total_count, missing_alt_count}, word_count, http_status_code, redirect_chain: [{from, to, status}], is_https, has_hsts}}`. Site-level rollup: `{duplicate_titles[], duplicate_meta_descriptions[], missing_h1_count, pages_with_noindex[], redirect_chains[{path, depth}], non_https_pages[], pages_with_broken_images[]}`. Feeds SEO lens (every prospect who's opened Screaming Frog expects this level of per-URL detail) + GEO lens (directives affect AI crawlability). Folds in image SEO alt-text audit + HTTPS/HSTS/security basics in a single primitive. `freddy detect <url> --full` already covers homepage-level DataForSEO technical audit for ONE page — this primitive is the same quality of analysis across all 200.
  - **`audit_content_quality(pages_cache) -> dict`** — Content quality audit (SEMrush Content Analyzer + Ahrefs Content Explorer parity). Same 200-page corpus reuse (no new HTTP). Returns: `{thin_pages[{url, word_count}] (threshold: word_count < 300), duplicate_content_clusters[{cluster_id, urls[], similarity_score}] (via simhash — deterministic + cheap, not embeddings), cannibalization_risks[{target_keyword, competing_urls[], recommendation}] (detected via title + H1 + first paragraph keyword overlap across multiple pages), stale_pages[{url, last_modified, days_stale}] (last-modified from HTTP Last-Modified header first, fallback to HTML meta — threshold: >365 days)}`. Feeds SEO lens (thin content and cannibalization are top SEMrush findings) + conversion lens (stale content correlates with declining conversions on content-driven sites).
  - **`estimate_traffic(domain, competitor_domains) -> dict`** — Organic + paid traffic estimation (Similarweb / SEMrush Traffic Analytics parity). Uses DataForSEO Traffic Analytics add-on (already budgeted in R7). Verification pass found that `freddy audit seo <domain>` subprocess is only a rank snapshot, NOT traffic estimation — so this is a real gap we close here. Returns: `{monthly_organic_visits_est, monthly_paid_visits_est, traffic_sources: {search_organic, search_paid, direct, referral, social, mail, display} as percentages, top_pages_by_traffic[{url, traffic_share, top_keyword}] (top 20), geographic_breakdown[{country_code, traffic_share}] (top 10), competitor_traffic_comparison[{competitor_domain, monthly_organic_visits_est, direction_vs_prospect}]}`. Feeds SEO lens (traffic trend context) + competitive lens (relative market position) + synthesis (Hero TL;DR can quote "~X monthly visits"). Graceful degradation on API quota / low-traffic-domain data sparsity → `partial=true`.
  - **`enumerate_brand_social_handles(domain, brand_name) -> dict`** (P19 — Phase 1) — Distribution-lens prerequisite. Parses rendered homepage HTML (reuses `RenderedFetcher` output from `tech_stack`) for `rel=me` links, footer social-icon `<a href>`, `og:*` tags, JSON-LD `sameAs`. For platforms not linked from the site, probes canonical slug patterns (`instagram.com/<slug>`, `linkedin.com/company/<slug>`, `youtube.com/@<slug>`, `tiktok.com/@<slug>`, `twitter.com/<slug>`, `threads.net/@<slug>`, `bsky.app/profile/<slug>.bsky.social`, `facebook.com/<slug>`, `pinterest.com/<slug>`) and validates existence via HEAD request. Returns `{instagram: {handle, url, exists}, tiktok: {...}, linkedin_company: {...}, youtube: {...}, twitter: {...}, threads: {...}, bluesky: {...}, facebook: {...}, pinterest: {...}}`. Feeds **P20 audit_channel_presence + P21 audit_youtube_channel** + **Distribution lens**. ~$0.05 infra (rendered-fetcher reuse + a few HEAD requests). No LLM. Graceful degradation per-platform.
  - **`audit_channel_presence(handles_dict) -> dict`** (P20 — Phase 2, depends on P19) — Organic-social cadence + engagement scorecard across owned platforms. Calls **XpozAdapter** for Twitter + Instagram + Reddit (profile-level: follower counts, posts in last 30d, engagement rates), **BlueskyMentionFetcher** (free Bluesky profile data), **ICContentAdapter** dual-instantiated (TikTok + YouTube creator discovery + content), **FacebookMentionFetcher** for Facebook page, **InstagramFetcher** (`src/fetcher/instagram.py`) for IG deeper profile scrape if XpozAdapter returns insufficient data. Returns per-platform: `{exists, handle, follower_count, post_count, posts_last_30d, avg_posts_per_week, content_mix: {photo, video, reel, carousel, text}, avg_engagement_rate, top_hashtags, branded_hashtag_detected, cadence_trend: growing|stable|declining, last_post_date, is_dormant}`. Feeds Distribution lens. Graceful per-platform degradation. ~$2–4 infra across 7 platforms.
  - **`audit_youtube_channel(youtube_handle) -> dict`** (P21 — Phase 2, depends on P19) — YouTube Data API v3 (free, 10K units/day). Returns `{channel_id, subscriber_count, total_views, total_videos, upload_cadence: {videos_last_30d, avg_per_week}, long_form_vs_shorts_ratio, avg_views_per_video, top_5_videos: [{title, views, published, is_short}], series_detected: [{playlist_name, video_count}], last_upload_date, is_dormant (>90 days), dormant_flag}`. Feeds Distribution lens. **Free** (YouTube Data API key from Google Cloud Console — env `YOUTUBE_API_KEY`). Graceful degradation if channel doesn't exist or API quota hit.
