  - **`audit_podcast_footprint(brand_name, execs[]) -> dict`** (P22 — Phase 1) — Detects owned podcast + executive guest appearances. Uses **iTunes Search API** (free, unlimited: `https://itunes.apple.com/search?term=<brand>&media=podcast&entity=podcast`) for owned-show discovery + **PodEngineAdapter** (owned) for transcript-level brand-name + exec-name searches. Returns `{owned_podcast: {title, show_id, episode_count, latest_episode_date, avg_episode_freq, apple_podcast_url, spotify_url, categories[]}, guest_appearances: [{exec_name, show, episode_title, date, host, episode_url}], sponsorship_mentions: [{show, episode, date, context}] (from Pod Engine with is_ad_segment=true)}`. Feeds Distribution lens. Graceful if no podcast exists.
  - **`capture_surface_scan(rendered_page) -> dict`** (P23 — Phase 1) — Lifecycle-lens public-signal audit **+ deep form-CRO sub-pass (extended 2026-04-22 — supersedes standalone audit_form_cro_deep proposal)**. Reuses `RenderedFetcher` output + a second Playwright pass with scroll + exit-intent simulation + **`_deep_inspect_forms()` sub-pass** that enumerates forms via `page.locator('form, [role="form"]').all()` and extracts per-form rich detail. Detects: `{popups: [{trigger: time|scroll|exit-intent|click, delay_seconds, incentive: pct_off|dollar_off|free_shipping|gated_asset|none, dismissable, selector}], embedded_forms: [{location: footer|pdp|checkout|blog|sidebar, form_intent: sales_demo|tofu_lead|newsletter|login, vendor (HubSpot js.hsforms.net / Marketo mktoForms2 / Pardot / Typeform / Tally / Formstack / Jotform / Calendly-inline), field_count_total, field_count_required, friction_score (required÷total with weighted penalty for tel/company/job_title on TOFU forms), fields: [{name, type (email|tel|text|password|select|checkbox|hidden), label, autocomplete (HTML5 token compliance per WHATWG spec), required, maxlength, pattern}], autocomplete_compliance_pct, is_multi_step (detected via data-step|aria-current|class*="step"|fieldset[hidden]), sso_options (regex match for "continue with google|github|microsoft|apple|linkedin|facebook|sso|okta|azure" + anchor href patterns `accounts.google.com/o/oauth2` + `github.com/login/oauth` + `appleid.apple.com/auth` + `login.microsoftonline.com`), captcha: {vendor (reCAPTCHA v2 `g-recaptcha-response`/`www.google.com/recaptcha/api.js` | reCAPTCHA v3 + `grecaptcha.execute` call | hCaptcha `hcaptcha.com/1/api.js` | Cloudflare Turnstile `cf-turnstile`/`challenges.cloudflare.com/turnstile/v0/api.js` | Friendly Captcha | GeeTest), version, sitekey}, honeypot: {detected, field_name, detection_method} (heuristic: `<input type="text|email|url">` with combined CSS hiding display:none/visibility:hidden/opacity:0/position:absolute;left:-9999px + common decoy names website|url|phone2|email2|homepage|nickname + tabindex=-1), inline_validation_wired (aria-invalid + aria-describedby + Parsley/VeeValidate/Formik/jQuery-validation listener detection), enterprise_gating_signals[]: [company_size_select, annual_revenue_select, contact_for_pricing, team_size]}], sms_capture: {present, tcpa_compliant (consent checkbox + rate-disclosure copy + double-opt-in)}, lead_magnets: [{title, url, is_gated}], preference_center_at_signup, welcome_offer_visible}`. Feeds Lifecycle + Conversion lenses. **Free**, infra-only cost. No LLM.
  - **`deliverability_posture(domain) -> dict`** (P24 — Phase 1) — DNS-level sending-hygiene audit via `dnspython`. Free lookups: `{spf: {present, record, syntactically_valid, qualifier (~all|-all|?all), include_count, lookup_count_exceeds_10}, dkim: {selectors_probed: [k1, s1, google, klaviyo1, selector1, mandrill], detected_selectors[]}, dmarc: {present, policy (none|quarantine|reject), pct, rua_reporting, ruf_reporting, aspf, adkim}, bimi: {present, record, has_vmc}, mx_provider, mta_sts: {present, mode}, tls_rpt: {present}, sending_domain_separated (e.g. mail.brand.com vs root)}`. Grading rubric in `conversion-lifecycle-agent-references.md`: `p=reject` is top-tier; `p=none + rua` is mid; no DMARC is red. Feeds Lifecycle lens + MarTech-Attribution lens (server-side / first-party signal). **Free**.
  - **`fingerprint_martech_stack(rendered_page, domain) -> dict`** (P25 — Phase 1, supersedes `detect_analytics_tags`) — Full martech inventory. Layered detection: (1) **python-Wappalyzer** against rendered HTML + headers (free, local, ~2500 fingerprints); (2) **custom regex ruleset** layered on top — catches reverse-ETL (Hightouch, Census — inferred from Segment destination config, subdomain CNAMEs, career-page mentions from owned `scrape_careers` output), HubSpot form IDs (`//js.hsforms.net/forms/embed/`), Marketo MunchkinId (`mktoForms2.loadForm`), Pardot iframe origins, Salesforce Web-to-Lead, OneTrust/Cookiebot/Iubenda CMP script ID patterns; (3) **network request host allow-list** against `network_requests` captured by `RenderedFetcher` (`cdn.segment.com`, `api.rudderstack.com/v1`, etc.); (4) **DNS CNAME inspection** for subdomained/first-party-proxied vendors (`metrics.<domain>`, `events.<domain>`, `trk.<domain>` often CNAME to Segment/Rudderstack/Snowplow). Returns per-category vendor inventory: `{analytics, cdp, crm, esp, sms, automation, ab_test, personalization, session_recording, chat, scheduling, consent, accessibility, loyalty, reviews, referral, subscription, search, cms, ecommerce, edge_network, payments}` with each vendor as `{name, category, confidence, detection_method, version, deployment_mode}`. Derived "stack sophistication tier" (none / basic / ESP+SMS / full-lifecycle). Feeds MarTech-Attribution lens + Lifecycle lens + Conversion lens. **Free** (all local). Optional paid fallback to Wappalyzer API v2 / BuiltWith only if evidence of rendered-detection gaps after 5 audits (R17 discipline).
  - **`assess_attribution_maturity(martech_stack, analytics_tags, internal_links_corpus) -> dict`** (P2a — reasoning-only, Phase 2) — Not a detection primitive, a **reasoning layer** that consumes `fingerprint_martech_stack` + `analyze_internal_links` page corpus + existing `detect_analytics_tags` subset. Derives: `{server_side_tagging_tier (absent|sgtm_cname|fb_capi|both), consent_mode_v2_present, first_party_identity_capture (Segment identify | Rudderstack | Customer.io | anonymous_only), utm_taxonomy: {source_cardinality, medium_cardinality, campaign_cardinality, naming_consistency_score, orphan_utms_on_canonicals}, cdp_warehouse_signals (from DNS + career-page mentions of dbt/Snowflake/Fivetran/Hightouch), tool_overlap_flags: [{category, vendors[], is_bloat}], dormant_pixel_flags: [{vendor, last_detected_days_ago}] (from BuiltWith LastDetected if available; else from `fingerprint_martech_stack` script-present-but-no-events heuristic), accessibility_overlay_red_flag}`. One Sonnet narration pass turns derivations into lens-ready prose. Feeds MarTech-Attribution lens. **Free** (pure post-processing + one small LLM call ~$0.02).
  - **`audit_messaging_consistency(domain, brand_name) -> dict`** (P26 — Phase 1) — Brand/Narrative lens cross-surface positioning diff **+ copy-quality deepening (extended 2026-04-22)**. Fetches rendered HTML from homepage, pricing, product, about pages via existing `RenderedFetcher`; fetches LinkedIn company page / Twitter bio / Threads bio / G2+Capterra self-descriptions; extracts meta/OG/Twitter card descriptions; pulls historical homepage H1 snapshots from Wayback Machine CDX API at 6-month intervals. One Opus call per surface applies April Dunford's 5-component positioning rubric (competitive alternative / unique attributes / value / best-fit customer / market category); a second Opus pass scores cross-surface coherence. **Copy-quality layer**: per-surface readability metrics (Flesch Reading Ease, Flesch-Kincaid Grade, Gunning Fog, SMOG, Coleman-Liau, ARI, Dale-Chall — all via single `textstat` call pinned 0.7.4 with `py-readability-metrics` fallback documented); jargon density via static buzzword corpus `src/audit/data/jargon_corpus.yaml` (~300 buzzwords across SaaS/marketing/AI — "synergy", "leverage", "best-in-class", "next-gen", "AI-powered", "seamless", "frictionless", "world-class" etc.; quarterly review); benefit-vs-feature ratio via piggyback on existing Sonnet call (add one more output field rather than new call); headline-strength composite (length 6-12 words hero / 4-8 nav via Sharethrough guidance; specificity via spaCy POS + concrete-noun count; action-orientation via spaCy dep-parse for imperative-mood verb in first 3 words; clarity via Flesch-Kincaid ≤8); voice consistency via spaCy POS-tag distribution across surfaces (pronoun variance, tense distribution, imperative ratio, drift score). **CoSchedule Headline Analyzer API does NOT exist publicly; Sharethrough is a free web tool without API** — build composite locally. B2B-technical-audience caveat: enterprise security copy SHOULD score grade-12 because audience expects it — score against vertical-appropriate benchmarks not absolute thresholds. Returns existing fields **plus** `copy_quality: {per_surface: {flesch_kincaid_grade, jargon_density, benefit_feature_ratio, headline_score: {length, specificity, action, clarity, composite}}}, voice_consistency: {pronoun_variance, tense_distribution, imperative_ratio, drift_score (0-100)}, top_jargon_offenders: [{surface, term, count}]`. ~$0.32 infra (existing + ~$0.02 for added Sonnet field + free libs).
  - **`audit_executive_visibility(domain, exec_roster[], firmographic) -> dict`** (P27 — Phase 2, depends on `scrape_firmographics` exec roster) — humans-in-public footprint per executive **+ founder-led weighting extension (2026-04-22)**. Per-exec queries: bylined articles (SerpAPI site-restricted searches over LinkedIn newsletter + Substack + Medium + trade-pub `site:` queries), podcast guest appearances (**PodEngineAdapter** transcript-mention search broader + Podchaser GraphQL structured guest credits — deduplicate by show+episode+date), conference speaking (SerpAPI site-restricted over conference sites), "quoted in" press (SerpAPI News + Google News RSS filtered to Tier-1 trade pubs from the earned-media tier dict), Wikipedia presence (`wikipedia.py` provider — replaces deprecated ORES with Lift Wing `articlequality:predict`). **Founder-led weighting (new)**: when `firmographic.employee_count < 50` AND exec `is_founder == True`, weight founder signals 2.0× — founder presence matters disproportionately for early-stage orgs. Detect founder mode: X posting frequency via `XpozAdapter` (user-search on handle — posts/30d, posts/90d, avg engagement, follower count, verified, inauthenticity_score); founder-written blog ratio (scrape `/blog` index → author byline from `<meta name="author">`, schema.org `Article.author`, `.byline`, `.post-author` → count posts by founder vs total in last 12 months); founder keynotes/conference talks via SerpAPI (`"<founder name>" keynote 2025`, `"<founder name>" speaker site:youtube.com`, `"<founder name>" site:eventbrite.com OR site:luma.com`) + YouTube Data API v3 search `q="<founder name>" interview` videoDuration=long; founder press mentions via `NewsDataAdapter` (sentiment + source_priority already exposed); founder mentions in creator content via `ICContentAdapter`. **LinkedIn honestly limited**: no realistic free path; use SerpAPI `q="<founder name> linkedin posts"` for URL surfacing only; optional Apify `harvestapi/linkedin-profile-scraper` (~$0.05/profile) gated on `firmographic.employee_count < 50` AND founder-mode active. Mark `linkedin_data_quality: "good"|"limited"|"skipped"` — do not pretend to have data. Returns existing fields **plus** `founder_mode_active: bool`, `per_exec.{x_posts_90d, x_avg_engagement, blog_authored_ratio, founder_mode_weight_applied}`, `linkedin_data_quality`. Cost ~$0.20–0.50 + optional $0.05-0.10/exec Apify LinkedIn when founder-mode.
  - **`audit_content_strategy_shape(domain, sitemap_urls[]) -> dict`** (P28 — Phase 3, depends on `analyze_internal_links` page corpus) — portfolio-level content strategy analysis, not page-level **+ newsletter + glossary deepening (2026-04-22)**. Embeds all blog titles (OpenAI `text-embedding-3-small` — reuses existing `openai` dep), HDBSCAN or k-means clustering → pillar count + balance + cluster-size distribution. Format inventory: detect blog / podcast / newsletter / YouTube channel / proprietary research via SerpAPI queries for `"<brand> report" OR "state of" OR "benchmark" OR "index"`. Gated-vs-ungated ratio. Editorial cadence from Wayback CDX snapshots of `/blog` index pages (posts-per-month rolling over 24 months). Series/franchise detection. Persona mapping via one Opus pass. **Newsletter subscriber detection (new)**: path probes `/newsletter`, `/subscribe`, `/digest`, `/weekly`, `/inbox`; subscriber-count claim regex on subscribe-page DOM context (`join\s+(\d+[\.\,]?\d*[KMk+]?)\s+(subscribers?|readers?|professionals?|founders?|marketers?)`) — parse "Join 50K+ subscribers" → 50000 lower bound; **Substack** direct HTML scrape of `<brand>.substack.com/about` (the `substackapi.com` third-party service is NOT verified — do not use); **Beehiiv** detection via `{{active_subscriber_count}}` merge-tag rendering on public landing page (Beehiiv API OAuth-gated for owner accounts only); **SparkLoop** script `app.sparkloop.com` = directional ≥1K subscribers signal; **ConvertKit/Kit** form embed `app.convertkit.com` + `kit.com/<handle>` public profile; ESP fingerprint via existing `fingerprint_martech_stack`. Mark `confidence: "verified"|"claimed"|"inferred"` — never claim without cross-validation. **Glossary / encyclopedia marketing detection (new)**: path probes (`/glossary`, `/wiki`, `/dictionary`, `/terms`, `/abc`, `/encyclopedia`, `/learn/glossary`, `/resources/glossary`); sitemap analysis counting URLs matching `/glossary/.+`, `/terms/.+`, `/dictionary/.+`, `/wiki/.+`; per-entry SEO signals via sample top-25 entries (word count per entry with threshold >300 words = SEO-grade vs <100 thin); `DefinedTerm` / `DefinedTermSet` schema markup via existing `detect_schema`; per-term keyword targeting via existing `DataForSeoProvider` keyword research on top-25 entry titles → search volume + rank + aggregate total search volume captured; internal-link density per entry; CTA-back-to-product presence in glossary template (measures whether glossary is true SEO play vs vanity content). Returns existing fields **plus** `newsletter: {present, signup_url, claimed_subscribers, claim_text, hosting_platform: substack|beehiiv|convertkit|kit|mailchimp|sparkloop_participant|self_hosted_via_<esp>, confidence, evidence_url}`, `glossary: {present, index_url, entry_count, avg_word_count, schema_definedterm_present, total_search_volume_targeted, avg_rank_position, top_ranked_terms: [{term, volume, rank}], cta_present_in_template, programmatic_seo_score (0-100 — low when entry_count<25 OR avg_word_count<200)}`. ~$0.55–0.80 infra (existing + DataForSEO keyword lookup on 25 terms ~$0.05-0.25 + $0.00 newsletter since scrape-only).
  - **`audit_earned_media_footprint(brand_name, competitor_brands[]) -> dict`** (P29 — Phase 1) — PR narrative + tier, not just mention count **+ Wikipedia depth extension (2026-04-22)**. Tier classification of pub list via maintained pub-tier dictionary (`src/audit/data/pub_tier_dict.yaml` — ship with ~200 pubs across top 10 verticals). Launch-coverage detection via homepage Wayback diffs + changelog scrape. Award/accolade presence via SerpAPI (`"<brand>" award OR "named one of" OR "finalist"`). GDELT DOC 2.0 API for narrative themes + tone over 90 days. One Opus pass over top 40 articles identifies 2–3 consistent storylines. Competitor delta on 2–3 firmographic competitors. **Wikipedia depth (new, via `wikipedia.py` provider)**: article existence + URL; article length (bytes); reference count (parse `<ref>` elements in wikitext); citation quality breakdown by source tier (Tier-1 NYT/WSJ/FT/Reuters/AP/BBC/Bloomberg/Forbes/TechCrunch/Verge etc., Tier-2 trade pubs, Tier-3 blogs/press-releases, self-citations from brand domain — **reuses existing `pub_tier_dict.yaml`**); **Lift Wing ML Reference Quality scores** (`need` + `risk`) via Wikimedia Enterprise Structured Contents beta endpoint (replaces deprecated ORES — ORES deprecated Jan 2025, served via Lift Wing now at `https://api.wikimedia.org/service/lw/inference/v1/models/articlequality:predict` + `references:predict`, free tier with optional `WIKIMEDIA_API_KEY`); recent-edit cadence (revisions endpoint → count edits in last 30/90/365 days; days since last edit); image + infobox completeness; languages translated (`langlinks` parameter); talk-page activity (noisy — low-weight); **quality assessment class** via Lift Wing `articlequality:predict` (FA/GA/B/C/Start/Stub). Brand-name→title resolution handles disambiguation via action-API search + infobox `industry` field match against firmographic vertical. **~70% of B2B SaaS don't have Wikipedia articles at all** — `present=false` is the modal outcome; surface honestly. Returns existing fields **plus** `wikipedia.{ref_count, refs_by_tier: {tier_1, tier_2, tier_3, self, unknown}, ml_reference_quality: {need, risk}, quality_class, image_count, infobox_fields_populated, languages_count, languages[], edits_30d, edits_90d, edits_365d, days_since_last_edit}`. ~$0.50–1.00 (SerpAPI + GDELT free + Wikipedia free + optional Lift Wing free).
  - **`audit_partnership_event_community_footprint(domain, brand_name) -> dict`** (P30 — Phase 1) — combined primitive covering partnerships, events, AND community **+ press kit + status page + webinars deepening (2026-04-22)**. Scans site for `/integrations` + `/partners` + `/customers` + `/ambassador` + `/creators` pages; OCR/alt-text-parses customer-logo walls; detects co-marketing signals. Conference sponsor footprint via SerpAPI site-restricted searches. Owned events + community (Discord Invite API, Reddit `/r/<brand>/about.json`, Slack/Circle/Skool/MightyNetworks footer links). Affiliate-program detection. **Press kit detection (new)**: path probes (`/press`, `/press-kit`, `/media-kit`, `/newsroom`, `/news`, `/media`, `/brand`, `/brand-assets`, `/brand-guidelines`, `/about/press`, `/company/press`); asset signals on press page (logo downloads via `<a href>` ending `.zip|.svg|.png|.ai|.eps` with anchor text "logo"; screenshots; headshots in `/team/`, `/people/`; boilerplate `<p>` containing "About <Brand>" 100-300 words; press contact via `mailto:press@|media@|pr@` links); newsroom velocity from sitemap (`/press-release/` or `/news/` URLs last 12mo). **Status page detection (new)**: subdomain CNAME probes `status.<domain>`/`trust.<domain>`/`health.<domain>` resolved via dnspython — classify vendor by CNAME target (Atlassian Statuspage `statuspage.io`, getstatus.io / status.io, Better Stack `betterstack.com`, Instatus `instatus.com`, sorryapp.com, freshstatus.io, hund.io, cstate self-hosted); path probes `/status`, `/system-status`; HTML fingerprints (Statuspage `<meta name="generator" content="Statuspage.io">`, Better Stack footer, Instatus `<meta name="instatus">`); maturity signals (incident history, component count, subscription form, uptime % displayed). **Webinar series detection (new)**: path probes (`/webinars`, `/webinar`, `/events`, `/live`, `/livestream`, `/sessions`, `/workshops`); hosting platform fingerprints (Goldcast `*.goldcast.io`, Hopin/RingCentral Events, Zoom `zoom.us/webinar/register/`, Riverside `riverside.fm/embed/`, Welcome `experiencewelcome.com`, Demio `event.demio.com/ref/`, On24 `event.on24.com`, Livestorm `app.livestorm.co/p/`, BigMarker); series detection (count past + upcoming); cadence (mean inter-event days; require ≥3 events in last 12mo to mark `series=true`). Returns existing fields **plus** `press_kit: {present, url, logo_downloads_count, headshots_count, screenshots_count, boilerplate_present, press_contact: {email, form_url}, newsroom_velocity_per_year}`, `status_page: {present, url, vendor, uptime_displayed, incident_history_visible, component_count, subscription_available}`, `webinar_series: {present, index_url, platform_vendor, upcoming_count, past_count, cadence_days, formats[]}`. ~$0.20–0.25 (existing + SerpAPI fallback ~$0.05).
  - **`audit_aso(firmographic_app_info) -> dict`** (P31 — conditional: runs only when `scrape_firmographics` detects a mobile app OR desktop-app marketplace presence) — App Store Optimization parity vs Sensor Tower / data.ai **+ 6-dimension weighted rubric + desktop marketplaces deepening (2026-04-22)**. For each detected app: pulls App Store listing via iTunes Search API (free, unlimited) + Play Store listing via existing `PlayStoreAdapter` (Apify). **6-dimension weighted scoring** (rubric codified in `src/audit/data/aso_benchmarks.yaml`): Title 20% (char count ≤30 iOS/Play, primary keyword in first 25 chars, brand presence, iOS subtitle utilization), Description 15% (char count vs 4000 limit, first-3-line hook quality, keyword density without stuffing, localization count, benefit-vs-feature via Sonnet), Visual 25% (screenshot count max 10 iOS/8 Play, video preview, screenshot type mix UI/lifestyle/feature-call-out, aspect-ratio compliance, localized variants), Ratings 20% (avg rating target ≥4.4, review count, velocity last 30d, developer-response rate, recent-review sentiment trend), Metadata 10% (category + subcategory, IAP listing depth, iOS promotional text 170 chars refreshable, iOS keywords 100 chars, Play short description 80 chars), Conversion 10% (review count ÷ days-listed, ranking trajectory, featured/editor's-choice badge, "most downloaded in category"). **Brand-maturity tier adjustment** (Dominant >10M reviews = ceiling-pushing focus; Established 100K-10M = standard weights; Challenger <100K = Visual/Description bumped to 30%/25% — acquisition stage). **Desktop marketplaces (new)**: Mac App Store via `parseforge/mac-app-store-scraper` Apify actor OR `facundoolano/app-store-scraper` Python lib (free, Mac App Store + iTunes coverage) when detected; Microsoft Store public scrape via `RenderedFetcher` (DOM pages at `apps.microsoft.com/store/detail/<id>`); Setapp via `setapp.com/apps` catalog scrape. **AppFollow/data.ai NOT required for this rubric** — iTunes Search API + existing Apify adapters cover all 6 dimensions; paid tools needed only for top-100 keyword rank / share-of-voice across 1000+ keywords which is beyond this primitive's scope. Returns per-platform `{title_score, description_score, visual_score, ratings_score, metadata_score, conversion_score, overall_score (weighted sum), benchmark_gaps[]}` + `brand_maturity_tier ∈ {dominant, established, challenger}` + desktop-platform entries. Cost ~$0.30–0.80 (Apify CU iOS + Android + 1 Sonnet rubric call + optional Mac/Windows ~$0.05).
- Modify `pyproject.toml`: add `playwright>=1.45.0`, **`wappalyzer>=0.4.0`** (s0md3v fork, supersedes unmaintained `python-Wappalyzer` chorsley fork), `beautifulsoup4>=4.12.0` (for `analyze_internal_links` HTML parsing), `dnspython>=2.6.0` (for `deliverability_posture` + `fingerprint_martech_stack` CNAME inspection + status-page CNAME + customer-education subdomain probes), `google-api-python-client>=2.0.0` (for `audit_youtube_channel` — same dep GSC already uses, so not net-new infra), `hdbscan>=0.8.40` (for `audit_content_strategy_shape` blog-title clustering + `audit_winloss` theme clustering; `scikit-learn>=1.4.0` already in deps provides k-means fallback). **2026-04-22 expansion R1 adds**: **`textstat==0.7.4`** (pinned — PyPI "Inactive"-flagged but functional; quarterly review; `py-readability-metrics>=1.5.0` as documented fallback path), **`spacy>=3.7.0`** + `en_core_web_sm` model (~50MB, downloaded post-install) for headline-strength + voice-consistency scoring in `audit_messaging_consistency`, **`axe-playwright-python>=0.1.4`** (Pamela Fox, actively maintained; injects axe-core via Playwright, ~90 a11y rules vs Lighthouse ~45) for `audit_accessibility`, **`python-pptx>=0.6.23`** for R22 deck parsing (already in plan), **`stripe>=7.0.0`** existing, **`pypdf>=4.0.0`** OR `pdfplumber>=0.11.0` for R26 win-loss transcript parsing (PyMuPDF already in deps via pymupdf). **2026-04-22 expansion R2 adds**: **`imagehash>=4.3.1`** (pHash for `audit_rebrand_history` logo-evolution diff via Wayback historical hero images), **`praw>=7.7.0`** (Python Reddit API Wrapper for `audit_reddit_ama_brand_subreddit` — handles OAuth + rate-limit backoff), **`feedparser>=6.0.0`** (Atom/RSS parsing for `audit_status_page_maturity` Statuspage `/history.atom` + Better Stack `/feed`), **`huggingface-hub>=0.20.0`** (lightweight HF Hub client for `audit_huggingface_presence` — alternative to direct httpx for token handling), **`email>=6.0.0`** stdlib (already in stdlib — used for raw .eml header parsing in `audit_welcome_email_signup` DKIM/SPF/DMARC alignment check). DataForSEO calls use existing `src/providers/dataforseo.py` client (extended with `audit_hreflang()`, `business_data_gbp()`, `local_pack_serp()`, `serp_site_query()` methods). Google PageSpeed Insights + internal-link crawl + SerpAPI + Wayback + Wikipedia + Lift Wing + GDELT + Discord Invite + Reddit + Podchaser + iTunes Search + GitHub REST/GraphQL + Product Hunt GraphQL + crt.sh + Firefox AMO + Atlassian Marketplace + Mozilla HTTP Observatory v2 + ATS public APIs (Greenhouse/Lever/Ashby/Workable) + npm registry + PyPI JSON all use `httpx` directly — no new dependency beyond the above. Bright Data Glassdoor scraper via REST API (httpx); Apify scrapers via existing `_common.py` Apify wrapper.
- Environment: `PAGESPEED_API_KEY` added to required env for `audit_page_speed` + `audit_accessibility` (free key from Google Cloud Console — extend with `category=accessibility`). **`YOUTUBE_API_KEY`** added to required env for `audit_youtube_channel` (free key from same Cloud Console project). **`SERPAPI_KEY`** added to required env for `audit_earned_media_footprint` + `audit_executive_visibility` + content-strategy proprietary-research queries + `audit_corporate_responsibility` PDF discovery + `audit_directory_presence`/`audit_marketplace_listings` overflow `site:` queries when DataForSEO miss-rates (~$130/mo upgraded tier covers expanded volume). **`PODCHASER_API_KEY`** added to required env for `audit_executive_visibility` guest-appearance per-person lookups (free tier). **2026-04-22 expansion R1 adds**: **`GITHUB_TOKEN`** required env (free PAT, 5K req/hr authed) for `audit_oss_footprint` + `audit_devex` + `audit_launch_cadence` + `audit_free_tools` + `audit_github_discussions_volume` (extended R2); **`PRODUCT_HUNT_TOKEN`** required env (free OAuth client-credentials at `producthunt.com/v2/oauth/applications`) for `audit_directory_presence` + `audit_launch_cadence`; **`WIKIMEDIA_API_KEY`** optional env (free tier signup at `api.wikimedia.org`) for `audit_earned_media_footprint` Lift Wing reference-quality scoring; **`BRIGHTDATA_API_KEY`** optional env for Tier-2 Glassdoor escalation in `scrape_careers` (~$0.10-0.50/audit, only for >$10M revenue prospects). **2026-04-22 expansion R2 adds**: **`REDDIT_CLIENT_ID` + `REDDIT_CLIENT_SECRET`** required env for `audit_reddit_ama_brand_subreddit` (Reddit free unauthenticated API formally degraded 2026; OAuth client-credentials free tier sufficient at ~20 audits/month; one-time ~30min app setup at `reddit.com/prefs/apps`); **`HUGGINGFACE_TOKEN`** optional env (raises HF Hub API rate-limit ceiling for PRO/Team/Enterprise tier — not required at <50 audits/hour) for `audit_huggingface_presence`; **`MAILINATOR_API_TOKEN`** optional env for private Mailinator domain ($99/mo, eliminates disposable-email blocklist issues at scale for `audit_welcome_email_signup` — public Mailinator inbox API is free but ~50-60% signup success rate due to ToS-blocked disposable domains). **Optional OAuth tokens for conditional enrichments (R19–R22)**: `KLAVIYO_API_KEY` / `MAILCHIMP_API_KEY` / `CUSTOMERIO_API_KEY` / `HUBSPOT_API_KEY` / `BRAZE_API_KEY` / `GOOGLE_ADS_OAUTH_TOKEN` / `META_ADS_OAUTH_TOKEN` / `LINKEDIN_ADS_OAUTH_TOKEN` / `TIKTOK_ADS_OAUTH_TOKEN` — per-client, stored in `clients/<slug>/audit/enrichments.json` (not global env).
- Create data files: `src/audit/data/pub_tier_dict.yaml` (~200 pubs across top 10 verticals — Tier-1 flagship / Tier-2 trade / Tier-3 syndicate; iterate after first 5 audits); `src/audit/data/conf_list.yaml` (major category conferences per vertical; lazy-built per-prospect-vertical); **2026-04-22 expansion**: `src/audit/data/martech_rules.yaml` (extended Wappalyzer ruleset — see Module Layout for category list); `src/audit/data/jargon_corpus.yaml` (~300 buzzwords for copy-quality scoring; quarterly review); `src/audit/data/budget_benchmarks.yaml` (R24 Gartner/OpenView/High Alpha benchmarks vertical+ARR-band keyed); `src/audit/data/crm_benchmarks.yaml` (R25 First Page Sage/OpenView/ICONIQ benchmarks); `src/audit/data/aso_benchmarks.yaml` (P31 6-dim weighted rubric + brand-maturity tier adjustment).
- Test: `tests/audit/test_primitives.py` — integration test hitting 2–3 real URLs per primitive

**Approach:**
- `RenderedFetcher.fetch(url)` returns a dict: `{url, html, ldjson_blocks, network_requests, status, render_failed, screenshot_path}`. Single browser context per audit (passed in); falls back to `httpx.get()` on render failure.
- Each primitive ~50–120 LOC, pure function, no shared state. Returns `{result: ..., partial: bool, missing_fields: [], cost_usd: float}`.
- Graceful degradation throughout: source unavailable → `partial: true`, no exceptions escape primitives.
- Shared LLM extraction helper (`_extract_structured(prompt, text, schema)`) for careers + firmographic scrapers — Sonnet with Pydantic output model.

**Test scenarios:**
- Happy: tech_stack on a Shopify store returns cms=Shopify + analytics list.
- Happy: enumerate_subdomains on stripe.com returns 30+ subdomains.
- Happy: score_ai_visibility for "notion" with 3 queries returns per-platform citation counts within $0.20.
- Happy: `analyze_backlinks("notion.so")` returns referring_domains > 1000 + non-empty top_referring_domains with rank/category fields populated.
- Happy: `audit_page_speed(["https://notion.so"])` returns both `mobile` and `desktop` nested entries with performance_score (0–100) + LCP/INP/CLS for each.
- Happy: `historical_rank_trends("notion.so", ["project management"])` returns a 6-month rank_series with at least some data points.
- Happy: `keyword_gap_analysis("notion.so")` returns at least 25 keyword_gaps with populated opportunity_score; top_competitors_by_overlap contains recognizable Notion competitors (Coda, Obsidian, Roam, etc.).
- Happy: `analyze_serp_features(["project management software"])` returns per-keyword dict with at least `featured_snippet`, `people_also_ask`, and `ai_overview` keys populated.
- Happy: `analyze_internal_links("notion.so", [...200 urls])` returns populated `orphan_pages`, `deep_pages`, and `link_equity_distribution`; `page_count_crawled` between 100 and 200 (respecting the cap); `_raw_pages_cache` populated for downstream primitives.
- Happy: `audit_on_page_seo(pages_cache)` returns per-URL title/meta/h1/canonical/directives/status analysis + site-level rollup with at least one duplicate_title detection.
- Happy: `audit_content_quality(pages_cache)` detects at least one thin_page + one duplicate_content_cluster on a known test site with intentional thin/duplicate content.
- Happy: `estimate_traffic("notion.so", [])` returns monthly_organic_visits_est > 0 + traffic_sources distribution summing to 100%.
- Edge: Crunchbase page 404 → firmographic returns partial=true + missing_fields.
- Edge: Cloro rate-limited → ai_visibility returns partial=true, cached data.
- Edge: DataForSEO Backlinks API credits exhausted → `analyze_backlinks` returns partial=true with the subset it fetched before hitting the limit; downstream lens proceeds with "backlink detail partial" flag.
- Edge: PageSpeed Insights returns 429 on a URL → that URL's entry is `{partial: true, error: "rate_limited"}`; other URLs' entries still present.
- Edge: prospect domain is brand-new (no historical data) → `historical_rank_trends` returns `{partial: true, missing_fields: ["historical"]}` and the brief notes "insufficient history for trend analysis."
- Edge: `keyword_gap_analysis` DataForSEO Labs quota exhausted → returns top 25 gaps + `partial=true`; synthesis proceeds with subset.
- Edge: `analyze_serp_features` called with 0 keywords (upstream primitives both returned `partial: true`) → returns `{partial: true, missing_fields: ["all_keywords"]}` without failing Stage 1.
- Edge: `analyze_internal_links` on a very large site (10K+ URLs in sitemap) → caps at 200-page sample, `partial=true`, `crawl_coverage_pct` populated so the lens can note the partial depth in its narrative.
- Edge: `analyze_internal_links` hit by robots.txt blocking → returns whatever was crawled before the block with `partial=true`.
- Happy: `enumerate_brand_social_handles("notion.so", "Notion")` returns Instagram + LinkedIn + YouTube + TikTok + Twitter handles with `exists=true` and resolved URLs.
- Happy: `audit_channel_presence(handles_dict)` returns per-platform follower counts + `posts_last_30d` + engagement rate for Notion (recognizable as the real org, not a spoof).
- Happy: `audit_youtube_channel("@notion")` returns `subscriber_count > 10000` + `upload_cadence` + populated `top_5_videos`.
- Happy: `audit_podcast_footprint("Notion", ["Ivan Zhao"])` returns owned_podcast=null (Notion has no show) + at least 1 guest appearance from iTunes/Pod Engine search.
- Happy: `capture_surface_scan(rendered_page)` on a known e-commerce site with a welcome-popup detects at least one popup with trigger + incentive populated.
- Happy: `deliverability_posture("notion.so")` returns SPF record + DMARC policy (`p=quarantine` or stricter on a reputable brand).
- Happy: `fingerprint_martech_stack(rendered_page, "notion.so")` returns ≥5 vendors across 3+ categories with confidence ≥0.7.
- Happy: `assess_attribution_maturity(stack, tags, link_corpus)` returns populated `server_side_tagging_tier` + `utm_taxonomy` + at least one derived flag (tool_overlap OR dormant_pixel OR cdp_warehouse_signals).
- Edge: `enumerate_brand_social_handles` on a domain with no social footer links falls back to slug-probing; platforms that return 404 are marked `exists=false` gracefully.
- Edge: YouTube Data API quota exhausted → `audit_youtube_channel` returns `{partial: true, missing_fields: ["cadence_detail"]}` with whatever it got.
- Edge: Pod Engine rate-limited on `audit_podcast_footprint` → primitive falls through to iTunes Search alone and returns `partial=true`.
- Edge: DNS query timeout on `deliverability_posture` → per-record `partial=true` without failing the primitive.
- Happy: `audit_messaging_consistency("notion.so", "Notion")` returns `per_surface` populated for at least 4 surfaces (homepage, pricing, LinkedIn, Twitter) + `coherence_score` between 0–100; `tagline_evolution_series` has ≥3 historical snapshots from Wayback.
- Happy: `audit_executive_visibility("notion.so", [{"name": "Ivan Zhao", ...}])` returns per-exec populated `bylines`, at least 1 podcast appearance, and Wikipedia lookup result.
- Happy: `audit_content_strategy_shape("notion.so", [...sitemap urls])` returns `pillar_count >= 2` + `editorial_cadence_series` populated with 12+ months + at least one `format_detected` beyond "blog".
- Happy: `audit_earned_media_footprint("Notion", ["Coda", "Obsidian"])` returns `tier_1` count > 0 + Wikipedia = present + at least 1 narrative theme extracted + competitor SOV comparison populated.
- Happy: `audit_partnership_event_community_footprint("notion.so", "Notion")` returns at least 1 integration partner + community presence (subreddit subscribers > 0 OR discord member count) + conference sponsorship detection.
- Happy: `audit_aso(firmographic_app_info)` on a known app returns populated `app_store` + `play_store` listings with rating_avg, review_velocity_30d, screenshots_count.
- Happy: `audit_aso` on a non-app prospect returns `{skipped: true, reason: "no_mobile_apps_detected"}` without failing.
- Edge: SerpAPI quota exhausted on `audit_earned_media_footprint` → falls through to Google News RSS only; returns `partial=true`.
- Edge: Podchaser free-tier rate-limit on `audit_executive_visibility` → falls through to Pod Engine transcript search only; returns `partial=true` for that exec.
- Edge: Wikipedia page doesn't exist → `wikipedia: {exists: false}` without failing the primitive.
- Edge: blog corpus < 20 posts → `audit_content_strategy_shape` returns `{partial: true, pillar_count: null, missing_fields: ["insufficient_corpus_for_clustering"]}`.
- Integration: all ~83 primitives run on one real prospect without exceptions; total wall-clock under 90 min (baseline 18–30 min + Distribution/Lifecycle/MarTech additions ~5 min + Brand/Narrative additions ~7–10 min + R1 expansion ~12–18 min + R2 expansion ~15–20 min — mostly Phase-1 parallelizable but conditional firmographic primitives may add 2-4 min each when triggered, deepening extensions add ~1-2 min apiece, GitHub-org-discovery in `audit_oss_footprint` is sequential to firmographic resolution, `audit_local_seo` Yelp/TripAdvisor Playwright fallback is rate-limited at 60s/site, `audit_industry_analyst_position` requires 6 SerpAPI queries serial to triangulate, `audit_welcome_email_signup` poll cycle adds up to 5 min for inbox check). ~16 conditional primitives skip cleanly when not triggered (typically 20-60% of audits trigger each): audit_aso, audit_local_seo, audit_oss_footprint, audit_abm_signals, audit_plg_motion, audit_devex, audit_international_seo, audit_corporate_responsibility (mid-market+), audit_vertical_compliance, audit_ecommerce_catalog (DTC), audit_b2c_personalization (B2C), audit_mobile_app_linking (mobile-app), audit_public_company_ir (public), audit_huggingface_presence (AI), audit_hiring_funnel_ux (ATS detected), audit_welcome_email_signup (free-trial + opt-in flag), audit_reddit_ama_brand_subreddit (when REDDIT_CLIENT_ID set).

**Done when:** Each primitive runs standalone from a python REPL against a real URL and returns a non-empty, schema-valid result. The 9 SaaS-parity primitives produce data comparable to Ahrefs / PageSpeed Insights / SEMrush / Screaming Frog / Similarweb. The 7 full-agency Distribution/Lifecycle/MarTech primitives produce data comparable to what paid-seat agency audit platforms charge $5K–$15K to assemble. The 5 Brand/Narrative primitives produce the narrative/positioning/PR/community-layer findings that separate a full-agency discovery document from a channel-specific audit. The conditional `audit_aso` (now with 6-dim rubric + desktop marketplaces) runs for mobile/desktop-app prospects and skips otherwise. The reasoning primitive `assess_attribution_maturity` produces derived maturity signals. **The 17 + 2 expansion primitives (P32–P48 + audit_plg_motion + audit_devex) run correctly per their conditional triggers** — `audit_international_seo` only on multi-locale, `audit_local_seo` only on local-business firmographic, `audit_oss_footprint` only on dev-tool/tech, `audit_corporate_responsibility` only mid-market+, `audit_abm_signals` only B2B-enterprise, `audit_plg_motion` only SaaS, `audit_devex` only dev-tool — and emit `{skipped: true, reason: "..."}` when triggers don't fire. The 6 deepening extensions (`capture_surface_scan` deep-form-CRO, `audit_messaging_consistency` copy-quality, `audit_partnership_event_community_footprint` press-kit/status/webinars, `audit_earned_media_footprint` Wikipedia depth via Lift Wing, `audit_executive_visibility` founder-led weighting, `audit_content_strategy_shape` newsletter+glossary, `scrape_careers` ATS+pay-transparency+LinkedIn-page+Glassdoor optional, `audit_aso` 6-dim+desktop) extend their parent primitive's output schema with new sub-signals without breaking backward-compat.

---

### U2.5. Cache-backed SDK tool handlers (`src/audit/tools/` — R5 addition 2026-04-22)

**Goal:** Build the 6 cache-backed SDK tool handlers that wrap existing wired providers, register them via `register_audit_tools()`, and ship the cache layer that makes Stage 1 → Stage 2 cost-efficient. Each handler is thin (~30-50 LOC). No new provider modules — every handler delegates to existing `src/seo/providers/`, `src/geo/providers/`, `src/competitive/`, `src/monitoring/adapters/` code.

**Files:**
- Create `src/audit/tools/__init__.py` — `register_audit_tools(state) -> list[Tool]` returns the tool list. Called by `stage_1_brief_sonnet` and `stage_2_agents` to extend each Sonnet `ClaudeSDKClient`'s toolbelt. Conditional inclusion: `gsc_tool` only included when `state.enrichments.gsc.attached==True`.
- Create `src/audit/tools/cache.py` — `read_cache(slug, tool_name, args, ttl_hours=24) -> dict | None` and `write_cache(slug, tool_name, args, result) -> None`. Cache files at `clients/<slug>/audit/cache/<tool_name>_<sha256(args)[:12]>.json`. Each entry: `{ts, args, result, error?}`. TTL check on read — return `None` if expired. **Tool-call `force=True` arg bypasses cache** (agent can request fresh).
- Create `src/audit/tools/dataforseo_tool.py` — wraps `src/seo/providers/dataforseo.py`. Exposes 8 tool methods: `on_page(url, max_pages=200)`, `backlinks(domain, type="referring_domains")`, `keyword_gaps(domain, competitors[])`, `serp_features(keywords[])`, `historical_rank(domain, period_days=180)`, `traffic_estimate(domain)`, `content_analysis(url)`, `hreflang(url)`, `business_data_gbp(brand, location)`. Each method: hash args → `cache.read_cache` → return on hit; provider-call on miss → `cache.write_cache` → return result; on provider exception, return `ToolError(diagnostic, retryable: bool)`.
- Create `src/audit/tools/cloro_tool.py` — wraps `src/geo/providers/cloro.py`. Exposes `ai_visibility(brand, queries[], providers=["chatgpt","perplexity","gemini","grok","copilot","claude","google_ai_mode"])`. Same cache + ToolError semantics.
- Create `src/audit/tools/competitive_tool.py` — wraps `src/competitive/service.py:CompetitiveAdService` (which already orchestrates `src/competitive/providers/foreplay.py` + `adyntel.py` + parallel fan-out + TTLCache). Exposes `ads(brand, platforms=["meta","google","tiktok","linkedin"], advertiser=None, include_variants=False)`. Cache-aware delegation.
- Create `src/audit/tools/monitoring_tool.py` — dispatches to existing `src/monitoring/adapters/*.py` via platform arg. Exposes 3 methods: `voc(brand, platforms[])` (fans out to Xpoz/IC/PodEngine/Trustpilot/AppStore/PlayStore/News/GoogleTrends/Bluesky/Facebook/LinkedIn/TikTok adapters), `press(brand)` (NewsData + GoogleTrends), `podcasts(brand)` (PodEngine + Podchaser overlay).
- Create `src/audit/tools/gsc_tool.py` — wraps `src/seo/providers/gsc.py`. Exposes `search_analytics(site_url, dimensions=["page","query"], days=90)`. Only registered when `state.enrichments.gsc.attached`.
- Create `src/audit/tools/types.py` — `ToolError` Pydantic envelope: `{tool_name, args_hash, diagnostic: str, retryable: bool, retried_count: int}`. Returned by tool handlers when underlying provider raises retry-exhausted; agent prompt instructs "on ToolError, retry once with `force=True`; if still error, emit a gap_flag Finding with diagnostic."
- Test: `tests/audit/tools/test_cache.py` (TTL, hash determinism, force=True bypass) + `tests/audit/tools/test_register.py` (conditional gsc inclusion) + per-handler integration tests against vendor sandboxes / VCR cassettes.

**Approach:**
- Tool registration is the only new SDK plumbing. Handlers themselves are ~30-50 LOC each because the existing providers do the work. Total new LOC across `tools/`: ~300.
- Cache key: `f"{tool_name}_{sha256(json.dumps(args, sort_keys=True))[:12]}"`. Deterministic in args. Sort_keys ensures `{"a":1, "b":2}` and `{"b":2, "a":1}` collide.
- Cache TTL: 24h default. Per-tool override possible (e.g., monitoring_tool.voc TTL 6h since mention velocity moves fast). Agent can pass `force=True` to bypass.
- Cache files are eval-harness fixtures. Eval harness (U9) freezes a `cache/` dir per fixture prospect; agent runs against frozen cache produce deterministic tool-call outputs (only Sonnet inference adds variance).
- ToolError pattern: tool handler implements 1 internal retry on retryable provider errors (network/5xx), then returns ToolError with `retryable=True`. Agent prompt instructs further handling.
- `register_audit_tools(state)` accepts state to support conditional inclusion. The tool list it returns is passed verbatim to `ClaudeSDKClient(tools=[*claude_code_preset_tools, *register_audit_tools(state)])`.

**Test scenarios:**
- Happy: `dataforseo_tool.on_page(url=X)` first call → cache miss → provider call → cache write → result returned. Second call → cache hit → result returned (no provider call). Unit test asserts provider mock called exactly once.
- Happy: `force=True` on second call bypasses cache, provider mock called twice.
- Happy: cache TTL — set entry ts to >24h ago, second call treats as miss.
- Happy: hash determinism across arg key order.
- Happy: `register_audit_tools(state_with_gsc_attached)` includes gsc_tool; `register_audit_tools(state_without_gsc)` does not.
- Edge: provider raises retryable error → handler retries once → if still fails → ToolError returned. Agent retries with `force=True` → if still error → emits gap_flag Finding.
- Integration: Stage 1 warmup populates cache; Stage 2 agents all see cache-hits for their initial tool calls; only drill-down calls add to cache.

**Done when:** A Stage-2 dogfood agent invocation pulls 5+ cache-hits for free and 2-3 drill-down calls that pay normal price; total Stage 2 cost is dominated by Sonnet inference, not provider calls.

---

### U3. Stages 0 + 1: intake + pre-discovery (cache-warmup + Sonnet pre-discovery + Opus brief — R5 2026-04-22)

**Goal:** Stage 0 (Python-only) populates workspace from intake form. Stage 1 restructured 2026-04-22 R5 from the earlier R4 hybrid (1a-Python / 1b-discovery-agent-with-primitive-registry / 1c-Opus) into **three simpler sub-stages** that align with the cache-backed-SDK-tools design:

- **Stage 1 (a) — Cache warmup (parallel Python, conditional).** `stages.py:stage_1_warmup` fires a conditional subset of `register_audit_tools()` calls in parallel via `asyncio.Semaphore(12)` to warm the per-audit cache (`clients/<slug>/audit/cache/`). Tool calls fired unconditionally: `dataforseo_tool.on_page`, `dataforseo_tool.backlinks` (prospect-only; competitor calls happen in U4 by Competitive agent), `dataforseo_tool.historical_rank`, `cloro_tool.ai_visibility`, `monitoring_tool.voc`, `monitoring_tool.press`, `dataforseo_tool.serp_features`. Conditional (firmographic-gated): `monitoring_tool.podcasts` when brand firmographic suggests thought-leadership surface; `dataforseo_tool.business_data_gbp` only when `business_type ∈ local_categories`; `gsc_tool.*` only when `state.enrichments.gsc.attached`. **B2C prospect skips** GitHub/SEC-EDGAR/HuggingFace URL-pattern hints in the downstream Sonnet prompt (not a tool gate — nothing in R5 fires those via Python). Also runs the 2 local-only helpers synchronously: `fingerprint_martech_stack()` + a cheap homepage Playwright fetch to seed `content_extractor`. Writes cached JSON via `tools/cache.py:write_cache(tool, args, result)`. Cost ~$0.50-2 depending on DataForSEO + Cloro quota usage, wall-clock ~60-120s.
- **Stage 1 (b) — Sonnet pre-discovery agent (default Claude Code toolbelt + tool list).** `stages.py:stage_1_brief_sonnet` opens ONE `ClaudeSDKClient` (model=sonnet) with `tools={"type":"preset","preset":"claude_code"}` extended by `register_audit_tools()` — agent gets full Claude Code toolbelt (WebFetch, WebSearch, Task, Bash, Read, Write, Grep, Glob) **plus** the 6 cache-backed SDK tool handlers. System prompt (`PREDISCOVERY_PROMPT`) briefs agent with: (a) the warm-cache manifest (tool_name + hash → path on disk, so agent reads cache directly via Read or via tool handlers which transparently cache-hit); (b) firmographic signals from intake form; (c) **explicit URL-pattern blocks** for all free public-API signals the agent may reach — GitHub (`api.github.com/orgs/{org}` with Bearer $GITHUB_TOKEN + User-Agent `GoFreddy-Audit`), Wikipedia (`en.wikipedia.org/api/rest_v1/page/summary/{brand_slug}` + Lift Wing `api.wikimedia.org/service/lw/inference/v1/models/articlequality:predict`), Reddit (`reddit.com/api/v1/access_token` OAuth with $REDDIT_CLIENT_ID/SECRET → then `reddit.com/r/<sub>/about.json`), SEC EDGAR (`data.sec.gov/...` + User-Agent with contact email required), HuggingFace (`huggingface.co/api/{org}` + optional $HUGGINGFACE_TOKEN), Product Hunt GraphQL (`api.producthunt.com/v2/api/graphql` OAuth client-credentials), crt.sh (`crt.sh/?q=%25.{domain}&output=json` with 1-req/sec polite pace), Mailinator (`api.mailinator.com/api/v2/domains/private` with $MAILINATOR_API_TOKEN if set), GDELT, Discord Invite API, Podchaser GraphQL, APIs.guru, Atlassian Marketplace, Firefox AMO, Mozilla HTTP Observatory, npm registry + PyPI JSON — each with polite-pace notes + pagination patterns; (d) **rubric-oriented investigation guidance** ("to seed brief sections for brand-credibility, investigate founder LinkedIn, Wikipedia article if present, industry-analyst position claims on brand site, Trust Center subdomain, press-page earned-media tier — decide depth per signal"); (e) explicit `gap_flag` instruction: "when data is absent or API blocked, emit a `{rubric, reason}` gap entry — do not skip silently"; (f) `fetch_with_retry` usage pattern (`cli/scripts/fetch_api.sh` shell wrapper — curl with exponential backoff, auth injection, pagination follow, User-Agent header — ~30 LOC). Agent explores adaptively, chasing anomalies, firing tool handlers that cache-hit instead of re-paying DataForSEO. Writes `signals.md` (prose notes, organized by rubric headings) + `gaps.jsonl` (one row per gap_flag with rubric + reason). Agent runs under `max_turns=600` sentinel (5-10× expected 30-90 turns), `permission_mode="bypassPermissions"`, `enable_file_checkpointing=True`, session_id persisted via `state.record_session("stage_1_brief_sonnet", result)`. Cost typical $2-6, wall-clock 6-12min. Hooks: observability only (PostToolUse loop-detect + token-spend alert + telemetry, PreCompact archive, Stop flush).
- **Stage 1 (c) — Opus brief synthesis.** `stages.py:stage_1_brief_opus` runs ONE Opus call (`PREDISCOVERY_SYNTHESIS_PROMPT` — unchanged structural role) against `signals.md` + `gaps.jsonl` + cache manifest + form data. Outputs structured `PrediscoveryBrief` (Pydantic envelope): ICP hypothesis with confidence label, inferred competitor list (reconciled from intake form + backlinks overlap + Foreplay/Adyntel shared ad-category competitors), pain points, tech posture summary, AI-visibility headline, hypotheses to validate on walkthrough. Writes `brief.md` (prose for Stage-2 agent consumption) + `brief.json` (structured). Cost ~$0.50-1. session_id persisted via `state.record_session("stage_1_brief_opus", result)`.

Stage 0 also loads any conditional enrichments present (GSC / ESP / Ad / Survey / Assets / Demo / Budget / CRM / WinLoss per R18–R26) from `clients/<slug>/audit/enrichments/` and surfaces them to downstream stages.

**Why R5 replaces R4:** R4's 1b "discovery agent with primitive_registry.yaml + ~65-70 tools" added a registry-selection layer that duplicated what the agent already does naturally when handed a warm cache + free-API URL patterns. R5's single Sonnet agent reads cache + explores via WebFetch — same coverage, simpler shape, same rubric discipline via prompt instructions. Agent adaptability + rot resilience + better edge-case handling preserved; reproducibility via cache fixtures + gap_flag discipline. A few primitives still need safety bounds (`audit_welcome_email_signup`, `audit_hiring_funnel_ux`, R23 attach-demo) — handled by **capability restriction + orchestrator pre-conditions** in `scoped_tools.py`, invoked as scoped sub-sessions from U2/U8 not from the Stage 1 brief agent.

**Files:**
- Create `src/audit/stages.py` with `stage_0_intake(state)`, `stage_1_warmup(state)`, `stage_1_brief_sonnet(state)`, `stage_1_brief_opus(state)` functions
- Create `src/audit/prompts.py` with `PREDISCOVERY_PROMPT` (Stage 1b Sonnet system prompt — rubric-oriented investigation + URL patterns + auth/pace blocks + gap_flag instruction + fetch_with_retry usage) + `PREDISCOVERY_SYNTHESIS_PROMPT` (Stage 1c Opus, unchanged structural role)
- Create `cli/scripts/fetch_api.sh` — ~30 LOC shell helper: curl with exponential backoff (3 retries, 2s → 4s → 8s), auth-header injection from env, User-Agent header, pagination follow-link handling. Used by Sonnet pre-discovery agent and Stage-2 agents for any free-public-API call.
- Test: `tests/audit/test_stages_0_1.py` + `tests/audit/test_stage_1_brief.py`

**Approach:**
- `stage_0_intake`: reads intake form data from `audit_pending` row (populated by Unit 7), writes `clients/<slug>/audit/intake/form.json` + `clients/<slug>/config.json` (prospect Client model). No LLM.
- `stage_1_warmup`: opens shared `RenderedFetcher` context; fires the conditional subset of `register_audit_tools()` calls in parallel via `asyncio.gather` + `Semaphore(12)`. Invokes the existing `freddy` CLI subprocesses (see list below) alongside for their specific payloads. Runs `fingerprint_martech_stack()` local helper synchronously. All outputs write to `clients/<slug>/audit/cache/<tool>_<hash>.json` via `tools/cache.py:write_cache`.
- `stage_1_brief_sonnet`: as described above — Sonnet agent with full toolbelt + cache-backed tools + prompt-mentioned URL patterns for free APIs.
- `stage_1_brief_opus`: existing `brief.py` pattern; Opus synthesis call over signals.md + gaps.jsonl → brief.md + brief.json.
- Existing `freddy` CLI subprocesses invoked from Stage 1a cache warmup (verified against actual code — descriptions reflect what each command actually returns):
     - `freddy sitemap <url>` → up to 100 URLs with `{url, lastmod, priority}`. Feeds page-corpus seed for Sonnet agent's investigation.
     - `freddy scrape <url>` → fetches one page, returns text + word count. Used for homepage hero text extraction.
     - `freddy detect <url> --full` → per-URL DataForSEO technical audit + PageSpeed Core Web Vitals for the homepage. Complementary to the dataforseo_tool.on_page tool for richer single-page detail.
     - `freddy audit seo <domain>` → **thin: DataForSEO domain rank snapshot.** Keep for rank snapshot.
     - `freddy audit competitive <domain>` → competitor AD data (Foreplay + Adyntel). Paid-media intel; competitive_tool wraps CompetitiveAdService for runtime access but this CLI is invoked for its side effect of populating the competitor brand-name list.
     - `freddy audit monitor "<brand>"` → recent brand mentions via Xpoz. Also covered by monitoring_tool.voc at runtime; this CLI populates the initial brand-name sweep cache.
     - `freddy visibility` subprocess **NOT invoked** — `cloro_tool.ai_visibility` supersedes.
     Each cache write keys by tool+args hash so re-invoking the tool at Stage 2 is a cache hit.
- Competitor discovery happens inside the Sonnet pre-discovery agent: it merges (a) prospect-provided competitors from intake form, (b) top-SERP overlap from backlinks cache, (c) shared ad-category competitors from Foreplay/Adyntel cache. Agent reconciles into a final ranked list of 3–5 competitors written to `signals.md:competitors`. Opus synthesis validates the list.
- Concurrency: Stage 1a uses `asyncio.Semaphore(12)` across cache-warmup tool calls + 6 `freddy` CLI subprocesses. Stage 1b is a single Sonnet session. Stage 1c is one Opus call.
- **No registry, no `primitive_registry.yaml`, no `agent_discovery_log.jsonl`.** Dependency graph is implicit: warm cache precedes Sonnet pre-discovery; Sonnet reads what's there and uses fetch_with_retry / cache-backed tools for anything else.
- Telemetry: per-tool-call cost/duration rows appended to `cost_log.jsonl`; Sonnet agent's transcript archived by PreCompact hook; `gaps.jsonl` captures every explicit gap the agent flagged (reproducibility substrate).

**Test scenarios:**
- Happy: intake form with URL → Stage 0 writes valid config.json + form.json.
- Happy: Stage 1 warmup fires conditional tool set (B2B-SaaS prospect triggers different set than local-business prospect) and writes `cache/*.json` under 2 min.
- Happy: Sonnet pre-discovery agent on a known prospect reads cache, WebFetches ~8-15 free public APIs per URL patterns in prompt, produces `signals.md` organized by rubric headings + `gaps.jsonl` with explicit gap_flags for any unreachable sources.
- Happy: Opus brief synthesis on full signals.md + gaps.jsonl produces brief.md covering ICP hypothesis + competitor list + pain points + tech posture + AI-visibility headline.
- Edge: cache warmup tool failure (e.g., Cloro throttled, DataForSEO 503) → `cache/<tool>_<hash>.json` contains `{"error": "...", "ts": ...}`; Sonnet agent reads error, retries via tool handler (with `force=True`), falls back to gap_flag if still broken.
- Edge: 10+ of the ~8-15 free-API calls fail (rate-limit / auth / pagination) → agent emits gap_flag per rubric affected; Opus brief flags partials in narrative and proceeds.
- Edge: Sonnet agent rabbit-holes → `max_turns=600` sentinel fires → Slack alert → JR reviews transcript. Also: PostToolUse token-spend alert (3× median) fires earlier, giving JR heads-up before sentinel.
- Edge: free-API auth env var missing ($GITHUB_TOKEN unset) → agent emits `gap_flag: "GITHUB_TOKEN not configured — oss_footprint unavailable"`; continues.
- Safety: Tier-D primitives (welcome_email_signup, hiring_funnel_ux, attach-demo) are NOT invoked during Stage 1 pre-discovery — they run as scoped sub-sessions in Stage 2 (invoked by Conversion-Lifecycle / Brand-Narrative agents per primitive rules) or from attach-demo CLI (U8). Scoped toolbelts via `scoped_tools.py` enforce capability restriction.
- Integration: `brief.json` validates against `PrediscoveryBrief` Pydantic schema; `cost_log.jsonl` has rows for warmup tool calls + Sonnet session events + Opus synthesis call; `gaps.jsonl` has one row per agent-flagged gap.

**Done when:** Running `freddy audit run --client <dogfood-prospect> --stage 1` produces a `brief.md` that JR reads and finds non-trivially useful without manual editing, AND `gaps.jsonl` records the agent's reasoning about what it could not reach (so quality-loss risks are explicit rather than silent).

---

### U4. Stage 2: parallel multi-agent analysis (7 agents → 9 report sections — R5 2026-04-22)

**Goal:** 7 Claude Agent SDK sessions (Sonnet) run in parallel via `asyncio.gather` with a `Semaphore(7)`, each producing a canonical `AgentOutput` with structured findings tagged by `report_section: Literal[...]` enum + a `rubric_coverage: dict[rubric_id, "covered"|"gap_flagged"]` map enforcing no-silent-skips. Restructured 2026-04-22 R3: agent count consolidated from 9 lens sessions to 7 strategic agents (SEO+GEO merged into Findability; Conversion+Lifecycle merged into one funnel agent); R5 2026-04-22: removed `rubric_themes.yaml` pivot table (findings route to sections via the Literal enum tagged by each agent), added evaluator-optimizer critique loop per agent (≤3 iterations), added cache-backed SDK tools via `register_audit_tools()` to every agent's toolbelt. Agent count and report count are decoupled deliberately.

**The 7 agents → 9 report-section mapping:**

| Agent | Report sections it produces | Why merged |
|---|---|---|
| **A. Findability** | SEO + GEO | Shared EEAT, robots, schema, content-authority signals; AI search is part of findability |
| **B. Brand/Narrative** | Brand/Narrative | Unchanged (~20 primitives — splitting Credibility from Narrative loses cross-cut coherence) |
| **C. Conversion-Lifecycle** | Conversion + Lifecycle | Unified funnel (visit→capture→convert→retain); shared `capture_surface_scan`, `audit_trust_signals`, martech-stack-slice signals |
| **D. Distribution** | Distribution | Unchanged (cohesive paid + organic + podcast + platforms) |
| **E. MarTech-Attribution** | MarTech-Attribution | Unchanged (specialized stack/attribution work) |
| **F. Monitoring** | Monitoring | Unchanged (VoC corpus = different data shape; pattern-clustering specialist work) |
| **G. Competitive** | Competitive | Unchanged (head-to-head competitor data fetching + comparison; not just synthesis) |

Each agent reads `brief.md` + `cache/*.json` (the warm cache from Stage 1 — any cache-backed tool call is a free cache-hit during Stage 2) and outputs `Finding[]` tagged with `report_section: Literal[...]` enum. Stage 3 synthesis groups findings by `report_section` directly — no pivot table.

**Files:**
- Create `src/audit/stages.py:stage_2_agents` function (runs all 7 agents via `asyncio.gather` + `Semaphore(7)` — each agent is an `async run_agent(agent_cfg)` call that executes: initial pass → self-critique pass → optional revision pass, capped at 3 iterations total)
- Create `src/audit/agent_models.py` (R5 rename from `lens_models.py`) — `Finding`, `AgentOutput` Pydantic models:
  - `Finding` required fields (R5 trim 13→6): `id`, `title`, `evidence_urls[]`, `recommendation`, `severity(0-3)`, `confidence(H/M/L)`. Optional: `evidence_quotes[]`, `reach(0-3)`, `feasibility(0-3)`, `effort_band(S/M/L)`, `category_tags[]`, `proposal_tier_mapping` (populated in Stage 3 after Stage 4 generates proposal tiers). **Required tagging field**: `report_section: Literal["seo","geo","competitive","monitoring","conversion","distribution","lifecycle","martech_attribution","brand_narrative"]` — the agent's declaration of which section the finding feeds; Pydantic rejects invalid values. The `recommendation` field is strategic, not tactical (unchanged from prior).
  - `AgentOutput` required field (R5 addition): `rubric_coverage: dict[str, Literal["covered","gap_flagged"]]` where keys are the rubric IDs for that agent's domain (drawn from the prompt's rubric checklist). Stage 3 validates that every rubric listed in the agent's prompt checklist appears as a key with a value of `covered` (≥1 finding produced) OR `gap_flagged` (explicit "insufficient signal" declaration) — a missing key is an invariant violation.
- Extend `src/audit/prompts.py` with 7 agent-specific prompts: `AGENT_FINDABILITY_PROMPT`, `AGENT_BRAND_NARRATIVE_PROMPT`, `AGENT_CONVERSION_LIFECYCLE_PROMPT`, `AGENT_DISTRIBUTION_PROMPT`, `AGENT_MARTECH_ATTRIBUTION_PROMPT`, `AGENT_MONITORING_PROMPT`, `AGENT_COMPETITIVE_PROMPT`. **Each prompt carries (R5 structural requirements):** (a) explicit rubric-coverage checklist — the 5-10 rubrics this agent must cover, each with evaluation-question + expected-finding-shape + which report_section(s) the rubric maps to; (b) per-API auth/rate-limit/pagination block for every free-public-API and owned-provider tool the agent may reach (e.g., "GitHub: `Authorization: Bearer $GITHUB_TOKEN` + User-Agent `GoFreddy-Audit`, 5K req/hr; SEC EDGAR: User-Agent must include contact email, 10 req/sec; SerpAPI: $SERPAPI_KEY; polite-pace 1 req/sec for crt.sh; etc."); (c) `fetch_with_retry` (`cli/scripts/fetch_api.sh`) usage pattern with explicit "on tool-error: retry once with 2s backoff, if still error emit a gap_flag Finding with error_diagnostics" rule; (d) **critique-loop instruction** — "after writing findings, re-read your own output and reject: findings with tactical (not strategic) recommendations; findings with weak evidence_urls or <50 words substance; findings with severity/confidence mismatched to the evidence. Revise and emit final. You get up to 3 iterations; a self-critique that passes on iteration 1 ships as-is."; (e) output contract — AgentOutput shape + rubric_coverage map expectation; (f) gap_flag instruction for insufficient-signal cases. Each prompt also injects `brief.md` + the cache manifest + matching `src/audit/references/<agent>-references.md`.
- Create `src/audit/agent_runner.py` — small orchestrator implementing the critique loop: `async def run_agent(agent_cfg) -> AgentOutput`. Pseudocode: `output = sonnet_call(initial_prompt); critique = sonnet_call(critique_prompt, context=output); if critique.passes: return output; else: output = sonnet_call(revision_prompt, context=output + critique); [repeat up to 3]`. Telemetry records `critique_iterations_used` per agent.
- Create `src/audit/references/` directory with 9 consolidated reference files:
  - Existing 4 (renamed for consistency): `stats-library.md`, `competitive-agent-references.md`, `monitoring-agent-references.md`, `voc-source-playbooks.md`
  - **Merged 2 (R3 restructure)**: `findability-agent-references.md` (merges former `seo-lens-references.md` + `geo-lens-references.md` — covers SEO technical, on-page, content-quality, backlinks, keywords, page-speed, intl/local, accessibility, EEAT, robots strategic, crawl-budget, conversational query, error page, Cloro positional metrics, AI Overview interpretation, Core Web Vitals benchmarks, AI-citation supply trajectory), `conversion-lifecycle-agent-references.md` (merges former `conversion-lens-references.md` + `lifecycle-lens-references.md` — covers page CRO, signup/form/onboarding/popup/paywall CRO, churn prevention, copywriting/marketing-psychology, Klaviyo/Omnisend/Customer.io 2026 benchmarks, TCPA SMS compliance, DMARC posture grading, ESP-granted-enrichment interpretation when R19 fires, capture-UX maturity bands, lifecycle-stack tier rubric)
  - **3 for full-agency lenses (renamed)**: `distribution-agent-references.md` (paid-creative teardown framework, hook taxonomy, offer patterns, UGC-vs-produced, channel-native-fit, podcast-presence interpretation, YouTube upload-cadence benchmarks, influencer-tier tagging patterns, **ASO grading rubric** when mobile-app detected), `martech-attribution-agent-references.md` (Consent Mode v2 interpretation, server-side tagging maturity tiers, UTM-taxonomy scoring rubric, CDP/ESP/CRM category definitions, accessibility-overlay red-flag context, dormant-pixel bloat thresholds), `brand-narrative-agent-references.md` (April Dunford 5-component positioning rubric, cross-surface coherence-scoring framework, pub-tier classification model — Tier-1 flagship / Tier-2 trade / Tier-3 syndicate, GDELT tone-reading heuristics, content-pillar cluster-balance thresholds, proprietary-research publishing benchmarks, editorial-cadence stability bands, conference-tier list per vertical, community-presence member-count tier interpretation, Wikipedia-presence reference-quality rubric, **client-asset-enrichment interpretation** when R22 fires — cross-asset consistency scoring)
- Test: `tests/audit/test_stage_2_agents.py`

**Rubric coverage discipline (R5 replaces rubric_themes.yaml pivot):**

Each agent's prompt carries a rubric checklist inline — the 5-10 rubrics that agent must cover, each with an evaluation-question, expected-finding-shape, and the report_section(s) each rubric maps to. Routing happens via the `Finding.report_section: Literal[...]` enum each agent tags, and coverage is enforced via `AgentOutput.rubric_coverage` (every rubric key must be `covered` OR `gap_flagged` — missing keys fail Stage 3 validation). Example slice of the Findability agent's inline rubric checklist (full text lives in `AGENT_FINDABILITY_PROMPT`):

```
Rubrics you MUST cover (emit ≥1 Finding per rubric OR mark `gap_flagged` in rubric_coverage):
- tech_seo_health                 → report_section="seo"   — Is the site technically healthy for crawlers? Look at on-page, internal-linking, content quality, page-speed, schema, robots strategic posture, crawl-budget bloat, error-page UX, schema-vs-competitor.
- link_authority                  → report_section="seo"   — Does the site have earned authority? Examine backlinks cache + branded-vs-commercial anchor-text distribution.
- ai_search_visibility            → report_section="geo"   — Is the brand cited in AI search; citation-supply trajectory? cloro_tool + robots_strategic posture + EEAT author-entity composite + HuggingFace downloads (when AI firmographic) + OSS footprint correlation.
- international_local_accessibility → report_section="seo" — Hreflang + GBP + NAP + WCAG when applicable.
... [~6-10 rubrics per agent, inline]

When you've produced findings, populate rubric_coverage with {rubric_id: "covered" | "gap_flagged"} for every rubric above.
```

Per-section health score is produced by Opus in Stage 3 with rationale (no weighted rollup).

**Approach:**
- `Finding` schema (R5 trim 13→6 required + report_section enum): **Required**: `{id, title, evidence_urls[], recommendation, severity(0-3), confidence(H/M/L), report_section: Literal["seo","geo","competitive","monitoring","conversion","distribution","lifecycle","martech_attribution","brand_narrative"]}`. **Optional**: `{evidence_quotes[], reach(0-3), feasibility(0-3), effort_band(S/M/L), category_tags[], proposal_tier_mapping, agent}`. Pydantic rejects invalid `report_section` values — routing is deterministic. Agent fills any count of Findings freely. **The `recommendation` field is strategic, not tactical** — it states *what would solve this* in terms the engagement delivers, not a DIY execution guide. Example (good): *"Enterprise landing pages lack schema coverage, suppressing rich-result eligibility for 8 of 10 tracked enterprise queries."* Example (bad — too tactical): *"Add Organization, Product, and FAQ schema with these JSON-LD snippets to /enterprise/."* Tactical execution detail is engagement work, not audit output. `proposal_tier_mapping` populated in Stage 3 synthesis once proposal is generated in Stage 4 — see U5.
- `AgentOutput` (R5 shape): `{agent_name, findings[], agent_summary, rubric_coverage: dict[str, Literal["covered","gap_flagged"]], critique_iterations_used: int, metadata{session_id, total_cost_usd, duration_ms, num_turns, model_usage, partial}}`. `rubric_coverage` is required — missing keys = invariant violation at Stage 3. `critique_iterations_used` records how many critique-loop iterations ran (1 if first pass passed self-critique; up to 3).
- Each Stage-2 agent: open `ClaudeSDKClient` with a **directive** `system_prompt` (role / objective / context / rubric-checklist / per-API auth blocks / fetch_with_retry usage / critique-loop instructions / output contract / termination). Inject `brief.md` + cache manifest + matching `src/audit/references/<agent>-references.md`. Agent decides depth per rubric using tool discretion. **Config**: `tools=[*claude_code_preset_tools, *register_audit_tools()]` — full Claude Code toolbelt (WebFetch, WebSearch, Task, Bash, Read/Write/Grep/Glob) **PLUS** the 6 cache-backed SDK tool handlers (dataforseo_tool, cloro_tool, competitive_tool, monitoring_tool, gsc_tool when attached, plus the cache module utilities). Cache-backed tools are cache-hits during Stage 2 for anything Stage 1 warmed; agent pays for drill-down calls only. `permission_mode="bypassPermissions"`, `enable_file_checkpointing=True`, `max_turns=500` (sentinel; normal runs 15-60 turns, merged agents up to 25-90), `model=sonnet`.
- **Critique loop** (`agent_runner.run_agent`): initial pass produces Findings + rubric_coverage → same-agent self-critique pass re-reads the output with the critique prompt ("reject findings with tactical recommendations, weak evidence, severity/confidence mismatched to evidence, <50-word substance; verify every rubric is `covered` or `gap_flagged`") → if critique passes, ship; if critique flags issues, one revision pass, then ship (passes or not). Max 3 agent-model calls per agent session (initial + critique + revision). `critique_iterations_used` logged.
- Hooks wired per agent: `PostToolUse` → loop-detection (hash `(tool_name, tool_input)`; Slack-alert on 5× consecutive, no abort) + telemetry + **per-agent token-spend alert (3× rolling median → Slack)**; `PreCompact` → archive full transcript to `clients/<slug>/audit/agents/<agent>/transcripts/`; `Stop` → flush `ResultMessage` telemetry to `cost_log.jsonl` and record `session_id` via `state.record_session`.
**Per-report-section content (which agent produces each section):** The narratives below describe what each of the 9 report sections covers. Per the agent → section mapping above: SEO + GEO sections are produced by **Agent A (Findability)**; Conversion + Lifecycle sections by **Agent C (Conversion-Lifecycle)**; the remaining 5 sections (Brand/Narrative, Distribution, MarTech-Attribution, Monitoring, Competitive) are each produced by their dedicated agent. Cross-cut signals (e.g. `audit_eeat_signals`, `audit_trust_signals`, `audit_oss_footprint`) are investigated by multiple agents (each pulls what it needs from `brief.md` + `cache/` + WebFetch); findings surface tagged with `Finding.report_section` enum per R5 routing.

- **Monitoring section** (produced by Agent F — Monitoring) consumes the full VoC corpus from `gather_voc` (10 owned adapters — see Data provider inventory) plus trend context from `GoogleTrendsAdapter` (breakout detection, related queries) and press narrative from `NewsDataAdapter` (`source_priority`, `ai_tags`). Findings surface: mention velocity trends, sentiment drift by platform, pain-point and praise clusters with direct `RawMention` URL citations, share-of-voice on high-interest queries, press-tier distribution (Tier-1 flagship vs Tier-3 syndicated-aggregator), podcast presence signal (owned vs guest appearances derived from Pod Engine show_name frequency + `is_ad_segment` filter), community footprint (subreddit presence from Xpoz), brand defensive perimeter (branded SERP + autosuggest + Reddit AMA). Does NOT duplicate Distribution section's structural-presence audit — Monitoring is the *narrative* layer ("what are people saying and where"), Distribution is the *footprint* layer ("do you have a handle there and how active is it").
- **Distribution lens** (new, full-agency coverage) consumes: (a) `CompetitiveAdService`-normalized Foreplay + Adyntel paid-ad corpus with `persona` / `emotional_drivers` / `creative_targeting` / `transcription` fields; (b) `audit_channel_presence` organic-social scorecard across 7 platforms; (c) `audit_youtube_channel` YouTube footprint; (d) `audit_podcast_footprint` owned + guest + sponsorship presence; (e) `NewsDataAdapter` press / earned-media corpus with `source_priority` tier classification. Lens findings surface: **paid-media creative strategy** (hook taxonomy, offer patterns, UGC-vs-produced ratio, landing-page congruence with ad promise, channel-native-fit, spend-intensity signal from ad volume + run duration); **organic footprint maturity** (present-or-absent × cadence × engagement-rate vs category benchmark); **video strategy** (upload cadence, shorts-vs-long ratio, dormancy); **podcast posture** (owned-show existence, exec guest appearances in trade-relevant shows); **earned-media tier distribution** (Tier-1 flagship vs Tier-3 syndicate). Does NOT re-litigate backlink / keyword / technical signals — those belong to SEO lens. Does NOT re-litigate sentiment — that belongs to Monitoring lens. Distribution is specifically the **channel + creative + cadence** layer.
- **Lifecycle lens** (new, full-agency coverage — MVP scope, flow-observation deferred) consumes: (a) `capture_surface_scan` popup + form + SMS-capture + lead-magnet data; (b) `fingerprint_martech_stack` lifecycle-slice (ESP / SMS / loyalty / reviews / referral / subscription vendor inventory); (c) `deliverability_posture` DNS hygiene (SPF / DKIM / DMARC / BIMI / MTA-STS). Lens findings surface: **capture-UX maturity** (popup timing + incentive vs Klaviyo benchmarks; exit-intent present; SMS 2-step opt-in TCPA-compliant; preference-center-at-signup); **lifecycle-stack sophistication tier** (derived from P25 — none / basic / ESP+SMS / full-lifecycle); **deliverability posture** (DMARC policy band, SPF-lookup-count health, BIMI + VMC presence); **retention-surface presence** (loyalty / referral / subscribe-and-save pages, reviews density on PDPs). Explicit scope caveat in every Lifecycle finding: "this audit cannot observe open/click/conversion rates without ESP access; those metrics are engagement-scope." **Flow observation** (welcome / cart / winback) is deferred to an optional 2-week supplemental report — too slow for the 3-day SLA — and is sold as an add-on at walkthrough-call time.
- **MarTech-Attribution lens** (new, full-agency coverage) consumes: (a) `fingerprint_martech_stack` full vendor inventory across 20+ categories; (b) `assess_attribution_maturity` derived signals (server-side tagging tier, Consent Mode v2, UTM discipline, tool overlap, dormant pixels); (c) `analyze_internal_links` page corpus for UTM-taxonomy mining; (d) `scrape_careers` mentions of dbt / Snowflake / Fivetran / Hightouch (CDP-warehouse-signal proxy). Lens findings surface: **stack completeness vs ICP** (a B2B prospect without a CRM form vendor is a red flag; a B2C prospect without loyalty / reviews vendors is a red flag); **attribution loop integrity** (client-side only vs server-side vs first-party-ID vs full closed-loop); **privacy + compliance posture** (CMP present; jurisdictional coverage gaps; DNT/GPC handling; dormant-pixel PII leak risk); **tool overlap / bloat** (multiple heatmapping / multiple chat / multiple scheduler = cleanup opportunity); **accessibility-overlay red flag** (AccessiBe / UserWay present = ADA-lawsuit-magnet flag). This is the lens agencies charge $15K standalone for — it's the single highest-leverage addition.
- **Brand/Narrative lens** (new, Option C full-agency coverage + 2026-04-22 expansion) consumes: (a) `audit_messaging_consistency` per-surface positioning rubric + coherence score + tagline evolution **+ copy-quality scoring (readability, jargon density, headline strength, voice consistency)**; (b) `audit_executive_visibility` per-exec thought-leadership output (bylines, podcast guesting, speaking, press quotes, Wikipedia) **+ founder-led weighting when employee_count<50**; (c) `audit_content_strategy_shape` pillar count + balance + proprietary research + editorial cadence + persona mapping **+ newsletter subscribers + glossary marketing depth**; (d) `audit_earned_media_footprint` tier-classified press + narrative themes + competitor SOV **+ Wikipedia depth via Lift Wing reference-quality scoring + article quality class (FA/GA/B/C/Start/Stub)**; (e) `audit_partnership_event_community_footprint` integrations + customer logos + conference sponsorships + owned events + Discord/subreddit/Slack/Circle/Skool community presence + affiliate-program detection **+ press kit + status page + owned webinar series**; (f) **`audit_customer_education`** academy/university/certifications/LMS-platform; (g) **`audit_public_roadmap`** Canny/Productboard/Featurebase + transparency score; (h) **`audit_corporate_responsibility`** ESG/sustainability/B-Corp/diversity/accessibility-statement (when mid-market+); (i) **`audit_customer_story_program`** case-study count + outcome quantification + video case studies + G2/Capterra review velocity; (j) **`scrape_careers` employer-brand layer** (Glassdoor when Tier-2, Indeed, Comparably culture dimensions, pay-transparency compliance — anchor finding for CA/NY/CO/WA jurisdictional violations); (k) optional enrichment from R22 client-asset upload + **R26 attach-winloss themes**. Lens findings surface: **positioning coherence**, **copy-quality vs vertical norms**, **thought-leadership index** (with founder-mode weighting for early-stage), **content-strategy maturity**, **newsletter/glossary asset class signals**, **earned-media tier gap + Wikipedia depth**, **ecosystem presence map** (community + partnerships + events + customer education + public roadmap + ESG signals), **customer story program quality** (hard-outcome quantification ratio), **employer brand + pay-transparency compliance exposure**, **brand-asset consistency** (when R22 fires), **win-loss themes** (when R26 fires).
